For example, this usually occurs within a Home Network containing multiple cPVRs in order to distribute storage of video, audio, and other data.

### A. 310

## 分级编码 hierarchical coding

Method to achieve different resolution layers on the decoder side.

### A. 311

## 分级块匹配 hierarchical block matching

A multi-level block matching algorithm which allows an increase in the size of the search area without causing an excessing increase in search time.

### A. 313

## 分解力测试图 resolution test chart

A television test pattern designed for checking the resolution of a television picture.

### A. 315

## 分量彩色电视系统 component colour television system

Colour television system in which the complete video signal is in the form of several separate components.

### A. 316

## 分配点 distribution point

A point where signals are taken from the trunk feeder or branch feeder to energize branch feeders or spur feeders.

### A. 318

## 分配链路 distribution link

Link designed to convey program signals from a program production centre to a transmitter or the head end of cabled distribution system.

### A. 323

## 分支馈线 branch feeder

Feeder for connecting a distribution point to spur feeders.

### A. 327

## 峰值音量表 peak program meter

An instrument designed to measure the peak levels of a sound signal, which has a short attack time-constant of a few milliseconds, and a long decay time-constant of the order of a few seconds.

### A. 330

## 服务质量 quality of service: QoS

Subjective and objective metric sets that quantify the performance of a network and its suitability for use with some applications and services.

### A. 331

## 浮雕效果 plastic effect; relief effect

An appearance of relief in the reproduced picture due to accidental or intentional modification of the video signal.

### A. 332

## 符号间干扰 inter-symbol interference: ISI

Distortion arising e.g. from group delay in single carrier modulations

### A. 334

## 幅移键控 amplitude shift keying

The instantaneous amplitude of the carrier is dependent of the logic level of the modulating data signal.

### A. 338

## 辅助时间码 ancillary time code

Time code information transmitted in the ancillary data space as defined in Rec. ITU-R BT.1364.

### A. 340

## 负极性视频信号 negative video signal

A video signal whose instantaneous value decreases when going from black to white.

### A. 342

## 负片效果 negative effect

Special effect in which the normal image signal is replaced by another image such that the instantaneous levels of the luminance signal are inverted symmetrically about a median grey level.

### A. 343

## 附加音频业务 additional audio service

A service containing channels to be added to the channels of the main service, such as commentary, or additional channels for enhanced sound systems as 3D TV.

### A. 344

## 复合彩色信号 composite colour signal

The colour video signal in systems which use colour subcarriers for the chrominance signals.

### A. 347

## 复合数字编码 composite digital coding

Method for the analogue-digital conversion of a colour television signal in which the conversion is effected on the composite colour signal.

### A. 348

## 复用 multiplex

A stream of all the digital data carrying one or more services within a single physical channel.

### A. 349

## 复用配置信息 multiplex configuration information

Information defining the configuration of the multiplex. It contains the current (and in the case of an imminent re-configuration, the forthcoming) details about the Services, Service components and Sub-channels and the linking between these objects. It is carried in the FIC in order that a receiver may interpret this information in advance of the Service components carried in the Main Service Channel. It also includes identification of the Ensemble itself and a date and time marker.

### A. 353

## 副瓣电平 side-lobe level

The ratio, in decibels (dB), of the amplitude at the peak of the main lobe to the amplitude at the peak of a side lobe.

### A. 356

## 覆盖区 coverage area

The area within which reception from a broadcasting transmitter is available under specified technical conditions, using household receiving equipment of currently agreed reference characteristics.

### A. 359

## 干线馈线 trunk feeder

<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="imgs/img_in_image_box_869_1327_905_1363.jpg" alt="Image" width="3%" /></div>


Feeder originating at the head-end of a cabled distribution system.

### A. 361

## 高端广播应用 high-end broadcast application

A broadcast application requiring a high amount of quality headroom in program production (e.g.: complex image post-processing).

### A. 363

## 高清晰度电视系统 high definition television（HDTV）system

A system designed to allow viewing at about three times the picture height, such that the system is virtually, or nearly, transparent to the quality of portrayal that would have been perceived in the original scene or performance by a discerning viewer with normal visual acuity.

### A. 364

## 隔行 interlace

The property of frames where alternating lines of the frame represent different instances in time. In an interlaced frame, one of the fields is meant to be displayed first. This field is called the first field. The first field may be the top field or the bottom field of the frame.

### A. 365

## 隔行比 interlace ratio

Interlace is a technique to prepare a picture for transmission by splitting up a video frame into two fields containing the odd and even lines of a TV picture. The ratio 1:1 describes a progressive format, where the input signal is frame-structured and not interlaced. The ratio 2:1 is used for an interlaced format, where the input signal is field-structured.

### A. 366

## 隔行场编码 interlace field coding

The coding mode used when the two fields of an interlace frame are coded separately. The pictures coded using this mode are called interlace field pictures, or field pictures.

### A. 367

## 隔行扫描 interlaced scanning

A form of scanning (in television) in which the complete picture is explored through successive fields. The lines of each field are scanned sequentially and are located between the lines of the preceding and succeeding fields.

### A. 368

## 隔行顺序 interlacing sequence

A series of numbers defining the time sequence of the separate fields, in interlaced scanning.

### A. 369

## 隔行因子 interlacing factor

Number of fields in each complete frame of the picture.

### A. 370

## 隔行帧编码 interface frame coding

The coding mode used when the two fields of an interface frame are coded together. The pictures coded using this mode are called interlace frame pictures, or frame pictures.

### A. 371

## 隔离距离 separation distance

The distance required between the borders (or peripheries) of two coverage areas served by either T-DAB services or by two different services.

### A. 372

## 个人录像机 personal video recorder; PVR

## 个人数字录像机 personal digital recorder: PDR

An end-user controlled device that records, stores and plays back multimedia content.

### A. 375

## 公共交织帧 common interleaved frame

The serial digital output from the main service multiplexer which is contained in the Main Service Channel part of the Transmission frame. It is common to all Transmission modes and contains 55-296 bits (i.e. 864 CUs).

### A. 376

## 公共信息业务 public information services

Public information services are specific un-associated Information Services. Examples of un-associated information services: news highlights, stock exchange, traffic conditions, sport results.

### A. 378

## 公钥证书 public key certificate

Data that is digitally signed for the purposes of verifying its integrity. Issuance of certificates may require a Trusted Third Party.

### A. 385

## 拐点 breakpoint

Defines the signal level above which the gamma law is applied (this is 0.018 of full scale for SMPTE 274M).

### A. 388

## 光电导摄像管 photo-conductive camera tube

A camera tube in which the photo-sensitive electrode is photo-conductive.

### A. 389

## 光电发射摄像管 photo-emissive camera tube

A camera tube in which the photo-sensitive electrode is photo-emissive.

### A. 391

## 光阀电视投影机 light-valve television projector

Television projectors in which the picture signal modulates a beam of light produced from a conventional light source, and an optical projection system.

### A. 397

## 光链路 optical link

Compact Disc Read-Only-Memory format, able to record up to 650/Mbytes of computer data (software, data files, multimedia products, etc.) on a 12-cm disc. The format includes a CD-ROM-specific directory/file structure allowing compatible access to files from a wide variety of hardware/software platforms.

### A. 402

## 光纤分配系统 optical fibre distribution system

Cabled distribution system using the technique of transmission by optical fibres.

### A. 406

## 光影像 optical image

The image produced, by an optical device, on the photosensitive surface of the scanning equipment.

### A. 407

## 光栅 raster

A predetermined pattern of scanning lines that provides substantially uniform coverage of an area.

### A. 408

## 光栅屏障式立体显像管 raster-barrier stereoscopic picture tube

Stereoscopic picture tube where a grid-shaped mask forms a two-way light splitter in front of the screen so that no further means (for example spectacles) are necessary for separating the two interleaved pictures for the left and right eyes.

### A. 409

## 广播 broadcasting

Radio communication in which transmissions are intended for direct reception by the general public; these may include sound programs, television programs, and other types of transmission.

### A. 412

## 广播电视发射台 broadcasting transmitting station

A centre for sound or television broadcasts, comprising one or more transmitters with their antennas and associated equipment. Examples: Radio transmitting station; television transmitting station.

### A. 414

## 广播电视频段 broadcasting band

A frequency band allocated to broadcasting by the Radio Regulations of the International Telecommunication Union.

### A. 415

## 广播接收机 sound broadcasting receiver

Radio receiver capable of reproducing programs transmitted by a sound broadcasting transmitter.

### A. 416

## 广播数据业务 radio data service: RDS

Broadcast radio information services transmitted as code and text using a 57 kHz subcarrier on fm transmissions. Contains information on radio broadcasts, and codes for automatic receiver control.

### A. 417

## 广播卫星业务 broadcasting-satellite service; BSS

A radio communication service in which signals transmitted or retransmitted by space stations are intended for direct reception by the general public.

### A. 419

## 广播信道 broadcast channel

A unidirectional broadband Broadcast Channel including video, audio and data. BC is established from the service provider to the users. It may include the Forward Interaction path.

### A. 421

## 滚动效果 scrolling effect

Special effect in which images appear to move, one after the other, sideways across the screen, or to roll smoothly upwards or downwards.

### A. 422

## 过渡区 transition region

The region between the Near Field and Far Field regions. Here the power density decreases inversely with distance from the antenna.

### A. 424

## 过黑 blacker than black

Zone where the level of a complete video signal is beyond the black level, outside the normal black and

white range of levels.

### A. 425

## 过取样 over-sampling

Choice of a sampling frequency which is several times greater (twice, four times, eight times, etc.) than the Nyquist frequency.

### A. 426

## 过去参考帧 past reference frame

## 过去参考场 past reference field

A past reference frame (field) is a reference frame (field) that occurs at an earlier time than the current picture in display order.

### A. 427

## 过扫描 overscanning

Excessive line and/or field sweep amplitude of the line scan or field scan relative to the nominal value resulting in the disappearance of picture edges.

### A. 430

## 行间转移式 CCD 传感器 interline transfer CCD sensor; IT-CCD

A form of charge-coupled device (CCD) used for image pick-up in video cameras. Electric charges created in the CCD cells (pixels) by the incident light are transferred pixel-by-pixel from the light-sensitive layer to an internal buffer memory from which a serial output signal is extracted.

### A. 431

## 行可见性 line visibility

A condition in which the line scan structure is visible to a normally positioned viewer.

### A. 432

## 行频 line frequency

Number of scanning lines traversed during one second.

### A. 434

## 行扫描 line scan

## 水平扫描 horizontal sweep

The movement of a scanning spot along the scanning line and the corresponding flyback.

### A. 435

## 行时间亮度失真 line-time luminance distortion

Variation in the horizontal direction of the luminance of the image of an object of uniform luminance.

### A. 436

## 行同步信号 line synchronizing signal

## 行同步脉冲 line sync pulse

A signal, generally a pulse or sequence of pulses, used to synchronize the line scanning process of the receiver with that of the television camera.

### A. 439

## 行周期 line period

The time taken for a single line scan, including fly-back.

### A. 441

## 黑白电视 black-white television; monochrome television

Television in which only the luminance of an object is reproduced and not the colour.

### A. 442

## 黑电平 black level

The level of a video signal corresponding to a specified minimum level of luminance.

### A. 448

## 恒定码率传送流 CBR transport stream

A Constant Bitrate (“CBR”) Transport Stream as used in this document shall mean a MPEG-2 compliant Transport Stream such that the rate of departure of packets from a hypothetical transmitter is constant with time. In the case of Ethernet-style networks, a hypothetical transmitter shall never experience a packet collision and all packets will be drained by the network at the rate sent by the transmitter.

### A. 449

## 宏块 macroblock

The four 8 by 8 blocks of luma data and the four corresponding 8 by 8 blocks of colour difference data coming from a 16 by 16 section of the luma component of the picture.

### A. 450

## 后处理 post-processing

Post-processing consists of two operations: deblocking and dering. Decoder can use either one, or both, of these operations to mitigate the effect of compression artifacts, and improve perceptual quality of video.

### A. 451

## 后肩 back porch

Portion of the line blanking interval situated after the line synchronizing pulse.

### A. 452

## 后期制作 post-production

The compilation of complete programs from recorded sound and vision sequences or individual shots by editing, signal processing, and the introduction of visual special effects or sound effects.

### A. 453

## 后向参考帧距离 backward reference frame distance; BRFD

As computed from syntax elements coded in the bitstream, this is nominally equal to one plus the number of frames between the current frame, and the subsequent (in display order) reference anchor.

### A. 454

## 后向预测 backward prediction

Prediction from the future reference frame (field).

### A. 455

## 后向运动矢量 backward motion vector

A motion vector that is used for motion compensation from a reference frame or reference field at a later time in display order.

### A. 457

## 互扰区 mush area

A region in which fading and distortion affect the reception from a sound broadcasting transmitter owing to interaction between ground and ionospheric waves from other synchronized sound broadcast transmitters.

### A. 461

划变 wipe

扫换 wipe

划像 wipe

A method of replacing one television picture by another, in which the boundary between the pictures is

caused to move progressively.

### A. 462

## 画中画 picture-in-picture: PIP

A display which can show two pictures at the same time; one is a normal picture and the other is reduced in size and superimposed over a part of the full-screen picture.

### A. 464

## 灰度电平 grey level

Video signal level which is intermediate between the black level and the white level.

### A. 467

## 灰度级失真 grey scale distortion

The incorrect reproduction of different levels of the grey scale.

### A. 468

## 恢复时间 recovery time

The time period between a physical interruption within the broadcasting chain and the achievement of full functionality.

### A. 471

## 绘图板 graphics tablet

Electronic surface upon which an operator can draw with an appropriate device, which provides a digital signal which can be converted to a complete video signal.

### A. 472

## 彗尾 comet tail

Impairment appearing as a tail following bright areas of moving objects, due to image retention.

### A. 473

## 混叠 foldover; frequency folding; aliasing

In the data-processing domain: Repeat spectra generated during sampling which fall within the spectrum occupied by the baseband samples making unambiguous interpretation of these samples difficult.

### A. 474

## 混叠分量 alias component

Mirrored signal component resulting from sub-Nyquist sampling.

### A. 475

## 混叠频率 alias frequencies

## 混叠区 alias zone

Disturbing digital signal components generated during sub-Nyquist sampling.

### A. 476

## 混合差分脉冲编码调制 hybrid differential pulse code modulation; HDPCM

A form of source coding combining differential pulse code modulation and other coding techniques.

### A. 478

## 混合终端设备 hybrid terminal device

An IPTV terminal device that can also receive content from different types of transmission systems (e.g. satellite, cable).

### A. 479

## 混响 reverberation

Persistence of sound decreasing with time in an enclosed or partly enclosed space after the signal from an

acoustic source is interrupted.

### A. 480

## 混响时间 reverberation time

Period of time taken for a specified decrease (usually 60 dB) in sound pressure level at a given frequency and point in an enclosed or partly enclosed space, after the sound signal from an acoustic source is interrupted.

### A. 481

## 混响室 reverberation room

A room specially designed to have a very long reverberation lime.

### A. 482

## 混音 mix

A method of combining two or more sources to produce a single source.

### A. 483

## 机顶盒 set-top box; STB

General term for an additional receiver external box for TV, e.g. digital TV receiver box.

### A. 484

## 奇偶比特 parity bit

A bit appended to a set of bits to make the sum modulo-2 of all bits always equal to "zero" or "one" NOTE-A parity bit is usually employed for the purpose of error detection.

### A. 490

## 基本流分量 component elementary stream

One or more entities which together make up an event, e.g. video, audio, teletext.

### A. 495

## 基色 primary colour

One of the three specified reference colour stimuli which permit, by appropriate mixing, the reproduction of various colour sensations, at least within a certain field. Note: In television the primaiy colours are, in general, red, green and blue.

### A. 496

## 基色图像 primary colour picture

Display produced by scanning in one of the constituent primary colours.

### A. 497

## 基色信号 primary colour signal

Electrical signal representing the luminance characteristics of the television picture weighted according to a specified spectral sensitivity curve.

### A. 498

## 基于 web 的电子节目指南 web-based EPG

An EPG that can be accessed on a web server by means of a URL.

### A. 505

## 级 level

A defined set of constraints on the values which may be taken by the parameters (such as bit rate and buffer size) within a particular profile. A profile may contain one or more levels. In a different context, level is the absolute value of a non-zero coefficient (see "run").

### A. 506

## 级联样式表 cascading style sheets: CSS

A standard describing style sheets for HTML document.

### A. 507

## 即兴按次付费 impulse pay-per-view; IPPV

A payment system allowing the purchase of access to individual programs without the need to select those programs in advance.

### A. 509

## 几何失真 geometrical distortion

Alteration of the geometric shapes of reproduced objects, including stationaiy objects. Examples: trapezoidal, S-shape, barrel, bowing, pin cushion distortion, etc.

### A. 510

## 几何失真测试图 geometry test chart

A television test card by which the geometric distortion of a picture may be assessed.

### A. 512

## 加密 encrypt:encryption

Secure a message or transfer, for example by means of a cipher.

### A. 513

## 加扰 scrambling

A process used to combine a digital signal with a pseudo-random sequence producing a randomized digital signal, conveying the same information, in order to facilitate transmission.

### A. 514

## 加扰电视 scrambled television

Television in which the original picture may only be reproduced by receivers with appropriate decoders.

### A. 516

## 加扰算法 scrambling algorithm

A mathematical process applied to a digital program signal to perform scrambling.

### A. 517

## 家长控制 parental control

Parental Control provides a mechanism for deciding the suitability of particular content for a minor on his/her age.

### A. 518

<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="imgs/img_in_image_box_127_1187_162_1219.jpg" alt="Image" width="2%" /></div>


## 家庭网关 home gateway: HG

The interface of the home network to provider access network.

### A. 519

## 家庭网络 home network: HN

A communication system designed for the residential environment, in which two or more devices exchange information.

### A. 521

## 兼容单声道信号 compatible monophonic signal

Program signal given when the left stereophonic signal and the right stereophonic signal from a stereophonic sound source are mixed, corresponding approximately to the program signal obtained from a monophonic source.

### A. 524

## 检错 error detection

Method of error control making use of an appropriate code in order to detect the presence of erroneous elements in a received signal.

### A. 525

## 检索 retrieval

Methods provided to query the index library. The most common consists of specifying the value of pre-formatted fields, like Title, Author, Production date, etc.

### A. 531

## 交叉交织 cross-interleaving

Process involving the formation of codewords before and after convolutional interleaving. Cross-interleaving provides error-protection against random bit-errors and burst errors.

### A. 532

## 交叉字奇偶校验 cross-word parity

A form of error-detection block code in which data is read into a two-dimensional array. Parity checks on the rows and columns allow the position of an error in the array to be determined.

### A. 533

## 交互广播 interactive broadcast

A digital interactive services mode requiring an active return channel in order for all its features to function properly.

### A. 534

## 交互节目指南 interactive program guide; IPG

A service navigation interface used especially for bi-directional interactive service with a server or head-end.

### A. 535

## 交互通道 interaction channel; IC

A Bi-directional Interaction Channel is established between the service provider and the user for interaction purposes.

### A. 539

## 校准抖动 alignment jitter

The variation in position of a signal relative to the position of a clock extracted from that signal.

### A. 543

## 接收机 receiver

The receiver is the device that receives a streaming transfer. The receiver may store the stream as is, convert it into another format, display the contents of the stream, or perform other functions.

### A. 547

## 接收控制 access control: AC

The process of ensuring that content is accessed only by those entities authorised to do so, and only in a manner for which they have been authorised.

### A. 548

## 接收控制系统 access control system; ACS

A particular set of rules for managing entitlement checking and conditional access messages.

### A. 550

## 接收准则 access criteria

CA system specific information needed by the ECMG to build an ECM.

### A. 552

## 节目交换中心 program switching center

Switching centre receiving program signals from various sources, and feeding them to other program switching centres, presentation control areas, or transmitting stations.

### A. 553

## 节目类型 program type: PTY

An identification number which can be transmitted with each program item to specify the type of program (news, classical music, etc.). 31 codes are defined.

### A. 554

## 节目类型名 program type name: PTYN

A extension of the PTY code which can be used to give more specific program type information, in the form of a descriptive text, than is contained in the basic numerical PTY code.

### A. 555

## 节目流 program stream; PS

A method of formatting data in the MPEG-2 system which is used to organize compressed video data into packets for delivery to down-stream systems. Program stream packets have variable length and are intended for use in relatively error-free environments (e.g. within a studio centre).

### A. 556

## 节目内容评估 program contents evaluation

The evaluation of the suitability for use of aspects of the program such as type of content, storyline, production values, suitability for audience types and age levels, etc.

### A. 557

## 节目片段码 program item number

A code compiled from the scheduled program time and the day of the month, which can be used to trigger the recording of pre-selected program items.

### A. 559

## 节目相关数据 program associated data: PAD

Information which is related to the audio data in terms of contents and synchronization. The PAD field is located at the end of the DAB Audio frame.

### A. 561

## 节目信息 program information

A data block containing information about one program event. It includes channel, times, ratings, themes, etc.

### A. 562

## 节目业务 program service

A Service which comprises an audio Primary Service component and optionally additional Secondary Service components.

### A. 564

## 节目映射表 program map table: PMT

Defined in ISO/IEC 13818 1. The PMT identifies and indicates the locations of the streams that make up

each service, and the location of the Program Clock Reference fields for a service.

### A. 567

## 解串器 deserialiser

Device which converts a signal from a serial data representation to a parallel representation (serial-to-parallel converter).

### A. 569

## 解码器 decoder

An embodiment of a decoding process.

### A. 570

## 解码时间戳 decode time stamp:DTS

An instruction to a decoder to decode a particular piece of information at a particular time.

### A. 572

## 解扰 descrambling

A process applied to a scrambled signal in order to restore the original signal.

### A. 577

## 紧急警告系统 emergency warning system; EWS

A feature allowing the transmission of coded warning messages (weather alerts, etc.) to special receivers.

### A. 578

## 近场区 near field region

Fresnel region of the main beam. The maximum value of the near field power density on axis depends only on power fed to antenna, the diameter of the antenna, and the efficiency of the antenna.

### A. 579

## 进入点 entry-point

A point in the bitstream that offers random access.

### A. 582

## 净馈送电路 clean feed circuit

A circuit by means of which the personnel at one of the sound program sources can hear the complete program except for their own contribution.

### A. 583

## 静态会聚 static convergence

Convergence achieved by the application of constant magnetic or electrical fields acting on each of the electron beams.

### A. 584

## 静帧 still frame:freezing

Picture derived from one or more fields, which is stored and which replaces the normal moving picture for a certain period.

### A. 587

## 镜像效果 mirror effect

Special effect in which the television screen is divided, so that part of the televisicin screen carries an image which is a symmetrical copy of the image appearing on the other part.

### A. 592

## 矩量法 method of moments; MOM

Method to calculate electromagnetic fields. It enables calculations to be made at both the transmitting and receiving ends, as well as in the near and far fields of the antenna.

### A. 594

## 聚光效果 spotlight effect

Special effect in which one part of the picture is made much brighter than the rest.

### A. 595

## 卷积交织 convolutional interleaving

A form of interleaving in which data is read into a two-dimensional array and each row of the array is delayed according to its position in the array. When data blocks are read from the array they are re-ordered. Convolutional interleaving is used in systems which do not have inherent data block structures (e.g. in compact discs, where data is recorded on a single spiral track).

### A. 596

## 卷积码 convolutional code

A coding scheme in which the content of a given data word at the coder output is dependent on several successive input words which, by the use of delays, are made available concurrently within the coder. Convolutional coding is suitable for data-streams which do not have an inherent block structure (e.g. digital audio data carried in a DAB transmission). Error propagation occurs if the coding is interrupted.

### A. 597

## 均衡脉冲 equalizing pulse

Pulse trains occurring just before and after the field synchronizing signal in some television systems; these are used to improve interlacing in the display.

### A. 598

## 均匀量化 uniform quantizing

## 线性量化 linear quantization

Quantizing in which all the quantizing intervals lying between the outer bounds specified for the two extreme quantizing intervals are equal.

### A. 599

## 均匀误码保护 equal error protection

An error protection procedure which ensures a constant protection of the bit-stream.

### A. 602

## 凯尔系数 Kell factor

In a television System using horizontal scanning, the ratio between the number of horizontal lines distinguishable in a picture to the number of scanning lines in the raster.

### A. 603

## 抗混叠 anti-aliasing

Correction intended to reduce the aliasing.

### A. 604

## 抗混叠滤波器 anti-aliasing filter

## 重构滤波器 reconstruction filter

Analogue filter at the output of a digital-to-analogue converter, used to reject frequencies above the required bandwidth.

### A. 605

## 颗粒噪声 granular noise

A visual defect, caused by quantizing and appearing as fluctuations of luminance and/or chrominance on uniform or nearly uniform parts of a picture.

### A. 606

## 可编辑单元 editable unit

The smallest portion of the essence container which can be edited such as a field or frame.

### A. 607

## 可变比特率 variable bit rate

Operation where the bit rate varies with time during the decoding of a coded bit stream.

### A.611

## 可分级性 scalability

Coding and decoding method for videos which supports the access to several picture qualities in a single data stream.

### A. 614

## 可选音频业务 alternative audio service

Programs which are intended to replace one or more of the main service channels, such as multilingual and hearing impaired.

### A. 619

## 空间混叠 spatial aliasing

A picture impairment arising because the number of display elements is insufficient to correctly represent the desired image.

### A. 620

## 空间内插 spatial interpolation

Interpolation to obtain the probable value of a signal at a given position (for example, in an image), on the basis of the values of two or more adjacent known samples.

### A. 621

## 空间冗余 spatial redundancy

Redundancy related to the likelihood that the characteristics of a pixel will be related to the characteristics of adjacent pixels in the same frame.

### A. 623

## 孔阑校正 aperture correction

Compensation for aperture distortion by increasing the levels of the high frequency components of the video signal.

### A. 624

## 孔阑失真 aperture distortion

Distortion produced by the finite size of the scanning spot and by imperfections in the associated optical paths, giving the effect of a reduction in the high frequency components of the video signal.

### A. 626

## 控制室 control room

Room associated with a television studio in which video and sound signals are processed, including such operations as level adjustments, switching of various sources, mixing and signal monitoring. It also includes various items of equipment required for the studio.

### A. 627

## 控制字 control word: CW

Data object used for scrambling.

### A. 628

## 块 block

An 8-row by 8-column matrix of samples, or 64 transform coefficients.

### A. 629

## 块码 block codes

## 分组码 block codes

A family of codes in which a source signal coded as m-bit words is converted to a channel code with n-bit words, with n greater than m. The number of possible n-bit words is greater than the number of m-bit words, so the words that are actually used can be chosen to achieve specific channel code characteristics (DC level, bandwidth requirement, etc.). A block code can also provide forward-error correction (FEC). A block code is used with a code book which relates m-bit words to n-bit words.

### A. 630

## 块匹配 block matching

Comparison of small areas (blocks of pixels) within successive frames of the digital picture sequence as part of a motion estimation system. The coder tests in turn all blocks within the search area and then identifies the block giving the “best match”. The spatial relationship between matching blocks is quantified by a motion vector.

### A. 632

## 快切 cutting

Continuity operation in which one part of a program is intentionally and suddenly replaced by another.

### A. 634

## 快速信息块 fast information block; FIB

A data burst of 256 bits. The sequence of FIBs is carried by the Fast Information Channel. The structure of the FIB is common to all Transmission modes.

### A. 635

## 快速信息数据信道 fast information data channel; FIDC

The dedicated part of the Fast Information Channel which is available for non-audio related Data services, such as paging.

### A. 636

## 快速信息信道 fast information channel; FIC

A part of the Transmission frame, comprising the Fast Information Blocks, which contains information necessary to configure the receiver, together with optional Service Information and data Service components.

### A. 637

## 快速信息组 fast information group; FIG

A package of data used for one application in the Fast Information Channel. Eight different types are available to provide a classification of the applications.

### A. 638

## 宽高比 aspect ratio

The ratio of the width to the height of a rectangular picture.

### A. 639

## 宽脉冲 broad pulse

## 半行脉冲 half-line pulse

Pulses, usually repetitive at twice the line frequency, a number of which collectively form the field synchronising signal.

### A. 646

## 扩展数据包 extended data packet

An ancillary data packet containing auxiliary data corresponding to, and immediately following, the associated audio data packet.

### A. 648

## 类 profile

A defined subset of the syntax of the standard.

### A. 649

## 立体电视 stereoscopic television

Three-dimensional television in which each eye is presented with a different picture corresponding to binocular viewing of the scene.

### A. 650

## 立体电视摄像机 stereoscopic television camera

Television camera for providing signals for stereoscopic television.

### A. 652

## 立体声编码器 stereophonic encoder

Equipment producing the stereophonic multiplex signal from the left-and right-hand stereophonic signals.

### A. 653

## 立体声电视 stereophonic television

Television in which the associated sounds are transmitted in stereophony.

### A. 654

## 立体声复合信号 stereophonic multiplex signal

The signal obtained when the left and right stereophonic signals are multiplexed.

### A. 655

## 立体声广播 stereophonic broadcasting

Broadcasting in which programs are transmitted with stereophonic sound.

### A. 656

## 立体声广播中的导频 pilot-tone in stereophonic broadcasting

A component of the modulating signal in the pilot-lone system at half the frequency of the suppressed carrier.

### A. 657

## 立体声技术 stereophony

A sound control, recording, transmission, or reproduction technique capable of providing the listener with a sensation of spatial distribution of sound sources.

### A. 658

## 立体声解码器 stereophonic decoder

Equipment for deriving the left-and right-hand stereophonic signals from the stereophonic multiplex signal.

### A. 659

## 立体声平衡 balance in stereophony

Adjustment of the relative gains of the channels conveying the left stereophonic signal and the right stereophonic signal so that the outputs of the loudspeakers will reproduce the original sound sources in their original positions.

### A. 661

## 连接允许控制 connection admission control

The mechanism that controls the traffic to be admitted into the network.

### A. 663

## 连续随机杂波 continuous random noise

The ratio, expressed in decibels, of the nominal amplitude of the luminance signal to the r. m. s. amplitude of the noise measured after band limiting.

### A. 664

## 联合立体声模式 joint stereo mode

The Audio mode in which two channels forming a stereo pair (left and right) are encoded within one bit stream and for which stereophonic irrelevance or redundancy is exploited for further bit reduction. The method used in the DAB system is intensity stereo coding.

### A. 665

## 亮串色 cross-colour

Appearance of spurious colour on a picture due to the luminance signals of a picture interfering with the chrominance signals of the same picture. Note: This impairment occurs particularly in systems using composite colour signals.

### A. 666

## 亮串色噪声 cross-colour noise

An unwanted colour effect on a picture due to the introduction of noise from the luminance channel into the chrominance channel. Note: This impairment occurs particularly in systems using composite colour signals.

### A. 667

## 亮度 luminance

The luminous flux of an elementary source in one direction, divided by the apparent surface area of this source in the direction being considered. Note: In the SI system of units the luminance is expressed in candelas per square metre (cd/m $ ^{2} $ ).

### A. 670

## 亮度通道 luminance channel; luminance path

Path followed by the luminance signal in a piece of television equipment.

### A. 671

## 亮度同步比 luminance-synchronizing ratio

The ratio of the white level to the synchronizing level, both with reference to the blanking level.

### A. 672

## 亮度系数 luminance factors

The proportions of the three primary colours needed to obtain the reference white.

### A. 673

## 亮度陷波 luminance notch

A filter inserted in the Iuminance path with the aim of reducing the cross-luminance in the decoder or the cross-colour in the encoder.

### A. 674

## 亮度信号 luminance signal

## Y 信号 Y signal

An electrical signal representing the luminance of the television picture elements.

### A. 675

## 亮度轴 luminance axis

The axis in chromatic space, containing the reference white, along which the luminance component is plotted, for any colour.

### A. 676

## 量化 quantize; quantization

A process in which the continuous range of values of an input signal is divided into nonoverlapping(but not necessarily equal) subranges, and a discrete, unique value is assigned to each subrange. A unique index is generated to represent this value.

### A. 679

## 量化电平 quantization level

The integer number attributed in the digital domain to a given quantization subrange.

### A. 681

## 量化失真 quantizing distortion

## 量化噪声 quantizing noise

The distortion of a signal resulting from the process of quantizing an original signal.

### A. 682

## 量化误差 quantization error

A measure of the severity of information loss caused by the attribution of discrete quantization levels to an analogue signal.

### A. 684

## 劣化平滑 graceful degradation

Method to avoid an abrupt degradation of the picture quality in the receiver.

### A. 690

## 零 分贝满度电平 0 dB full scale; 0 dBFS

The maximum signal level that a digital audio system is capable of representing. Above this level, abrupt signal clipping occurs with the consequent distortion.

### A. 691

## 零 符号 null symbol

The first OFDM symbol of the Transmission frame, used for basic synchronization in the receiver.

### A. 692

## 零 相位基准 zero phase reference

The positive direction of the axis of the U signal, in the PAL colour television system.

### A. 693

## 浏览 browsing

The operation that allows users to view/listen a preview of the material selected during retrieval, by accessing a low-quality copy of the program contained in the index library.

### A. 694

## 流模式 stream mode

The mode of data transmission within the Main Service Channel in which data are carried transparently from source to destination. Data are carried in Logical frames.

### A. 695

## 录播 recorded broadcast

A sound or television program which is transmitted after it has been recorded.

### A. 696

## 录像机 video recorder

Equipment for the recording and reproduction of television signals.

### A. 698

## 录制间 recording studio

A room containing the equipment required to record sound or vision program signals and to monitor the recording.

### A. 700

## 路由器 router

Equipment used to establish circuits between signal sources and destinations.

### A. 702

## 轮廓校正 contour correction

Subjective enhancement of picture definition by the selective increase in level of high frequency components of the video signal in order to accentuate the edges of objects.

### A. 703

## 轮廓特技 outline effect

Special effect in which only the edges of a televised object are reproduced.

### A. 704

## 轮廓现象 contouring

## 轮廓失真 contour distortion

The occurrence of jagged edges on digitally-processed images, seen typically as a “staircase” effect on diagonal edges. The severity of contouring is dependent on the number of quantization levels and on the sampling frequency.

### A. 708

## 马赛克效果 mosaic effect; pixelisation; pixelation

Special effect in which groups of contiguous picture elements are replaced by rectangles of uniform brightness and colour.

### A. 709

## 脉冲编码调制 pulse code modulation; PCM

A process in which a signal is sampled, each sample is quantized independently of other samples, and the resulting succession of quantized values is converted by encoding into a digital signal.

### A. 710

## 脉冲上升时间 rise time of a pulse

the time interval between the instants at which the instantaneous value of a pulse first reaches a specified lower value and then a specified upper value (note: the lower and upper values are usually taken as 10% and 90% of the pulse magnitude) (IEC-55-35-110).

### A.711

## 脉冲下降时间 fall time of a pulse

## 脉冲衰减时间 decay time of a pulse

The time interval between the instants at which the instantaneous value of a pulse again reaches a specified upper value and then a specified lower value.

### A. 715

## 描述性元数据 descriptive metadata: DM

Data which can be placed in the file to describe the essence.

### A. 718

## 模拟信号 analog signal

A signal in which the characteristic quantity representing information can at any instant assume any value within a continuous interval.

### A. 719

## 模-数转换 analog-to-digital（A/D）conversion

A process for converting an analogue signal into a digital signal with essentially the same information.

### A. 722

## 内容包 content package: CP

A generic term for a grouping of some combination of system, picture, sound, data and/or compound items.

### A. 723

## 内容包装 content wrapper

A logical layer accompanying the Content for the purposes of describing and/or protecting it, including without limitation Metadata, CA and Copy Protection. This is distinct from Watermarking.

### A.724

## 内容保护 content protection

The control of access to content and use through usage rights and rules.

### A. 725

## 内容保护和复制管理 content protection and copy management: CPCM

The means whereby rights owners can control the copying and/or re-distribution of content which is broadcast or otherwise distributed.

### A. 726

## 内容跟踪 content tracing

A process to enable the identification of the (arbitrary) origin of content, and/or the responsible party (e.g. the end-user), to facilitate subsequent investigation in the event of unauthorized content copying or distribution.

### A. 727

## 内容汇集者 content aggregator

A player in the IPTV service delivery chain whose role is to aggregate content, e.g. to form a TV bouquet composed of several TV channels.

### A. 728

## 内容库 content library

The part of the archive that contains and manages the media on which copies of the audio/television programs are stored and is thus responsible for the storage and preservation of the materials.

### A. 729

## 内容提供商 content provider

The content provider is the entity owning contents or being licensed to sell content assets. Their role is contents delivery.

### A. 730

## 内容项 content item: CI

A collection of one or more Content Elements, plus any Metadata directly related to the Content Item itself or required to associate the component parts (Content Elements) together—for example, a video clip.

### A. 731

## 内容元素 content element:CE

A part of the digital content that consists only of Essence of a single type, plus any Metadata directly related only to that Essence-for example, the blocks of samples of a video signal plus the Format Metadata describing the sample structure plus the Descriptive Metadata identifying the origin of the signal.

### A. 732

## 内载波伴音方式 intercarrier sound

A technique used in television receivers whereby the difference frequency obtained by non-linear combination of the sound carrier and vision carriers is used as the intermediate frequency in the part of the receiver which processes the sound signal.

### A. 734

## 逆程 flyback retrace

The return of the scanning spot from the end of a line or field to the commencement of the next.

A. 735

## 拍摄 shooting

The action of producing a picture of the scene to be televised and an electrical signal corresponding to the brightness and colour characteristics of the scene.

### A. 736

## 配音 dubbing

Production of a television program sequence in which the sounds are added after vision recording and sounds are adjusted in accordance with the visual content of the program shown on a screen.

### A. 737

## 匹配网络 matching network

A network that provides a transformation of impedance to a desired value to maximize the power dissipated by a load.

### A. 739

## 偏振光眼镜 polarizing glasses

Stereoscopic glasses where the separation of the pictures for the left and right eye is provided by two polarizing filters whose orientation of polarization is arranged at right angles to each other (linear polarization) or in opposite directions (circular polarization) or both.

### A. 740

## 偏振模色散 polarization mode dispersion

Polarization mode dispersion (PMD) is a form of modal dispersion where two different polarizations of light in a waveguide, which normally travel at the same speed, travel at different speeds due to random imperfections and asymmetries, causing random spreading of optical pulses.

### A. 741

## 偏转线圈 deflection coils

The assembly of coils and magnetic circuits disposed around the neck of a camera tube or picture tube for scanning purposes.

### A. 745

## 频分复用 frequency division multiplexing

Transmission of two or more data-streams on a single bearer, each modulated onto a carrier at a different frequency.

### A. 747

## 频率合成 frequency synthesis

A frequency synthesizer is an electronic system for generating any of a range of frequencies from a single fixed timebase or oscillator.

### A. 749

## 频率偏差 frequency deviation

Frequency deviation ( $ \Delta f $ ) is used in FM radio to describe the maximum instantaneous difference between an FM modulated frequency and the nominal carrier frequency.

### A. 750

## 频率容限 frequency tolerance

The maximum permissible departure by the center frequency of the frequency band occupied by an emission from the assigned frequency. The frequency tolerance is expressed as a percentage or in Hertz.

### A. 751

## 频率稳定度 frequency stability

The Frequency Tolerance of a crystal or oscillator is defined as the initial deviation of the crystal or oscillator frequency as compared to the absolute at  $ 25^{\circ} $ C.

### A. 753

## 频谱模板 spectrum mask

A mathematically-defined set of lines applied to the levels of radio (or optical) transmissions.

### A. 755

## 平板显示器 flat panel display

Computer or television screen that avoids the use of CRT technology in order to achieve a shallow physical depth.

### A. 756

## 平衡 balance

Balance can mean the amount of signal from each channel reproduced in a stereo audio recording.

### A. 757

## 平均图像电平 average picture-signal level; APL

The average video signal level during a picture period, excluding blanking intervals.

### A. 759

## 评论声 clean commentary

The commentary signal before mixing with the main program signal.

### A. 760

## 屏蔽耦合损耗 coupling loss; CL

Coupling loss also known as connection loss is the loss that occurs when energy is transferred from one circuit, circuit element, or medium to another.

### A. 765

## 前后比 front to back ratio

The ratio of power gain between the front and rear of a directional antenna.

### A. 766

## 前肩 front porch

The interval between the end of active video and the half-height of the leading negative edge of the tri-level sync pulse.

### A. 767

## 前向纠错 forward-error correction; FEC

Source coding techniques which reinforce the ruggedness of a data signal which will be subjected to a processing or transmission chain which may introduce errors.

### A. 768

## 前向纠错码 forward error correction code

A system of error control for data transmission, whereby the sender adds redundant data to its messages, which allows the receiver to detect and correct errors.

### A. 769

## 前向预测 forward prediction

Prediction from the past reference frame (field).

### A. 770

## 前向运动矢量 forward motion vector

Amotion vector that is used for motion compensation from a reference frame or reference field at an earlier time in display order.

### A.771

## 钳位 clamping

Holding the level of a defined part of the complete video signal at a specified value. Notes—1—Clamping is usually used to restore the DC component of a picture. 2—Associated term: to clamp.

### A. 772

## 钳位脉冲 clamping pulse

A pulse used for determining the part of the video signal to be clamped.

### A.774

## 强度立体声 intensity stereo

Intensity stereo is the technique used by a stereo sound image that is produced only by differences in volume between the left and right loudspeakers, rather than arrival time differences.

### A. 775

## 强度立体声编码 intensity stereo coding

A method of exploiting stereo irrelevance or redundancy in stereophonic audio programs. It is based on retaining only the energy envelope of the right and left channels at high frequencies. At low frequencies, the fine structure of the left and right channel of a stereophonic signal is retained.

### A.777

## 桥接放大器 bridging amplifier

An amplifier connected to a feeder, intended to energize one or more other feeders.

### A. 778

## 切换矩阵 switching matrix

A remote-controlled array of switches permitting the rapid rearrangement of interconnections between items of video (and/or audio) production equipment.

### A. 780

## 清晰度 definition

A measure of the sharpness of detail of a television picture. Examples: vertical resolution, horizontal resolution.

### A. 782

## 取样频率 sampling frequency

Frequency or rate at which samples are taken of the analogue source signal. The subjective quality of the reproduced image or sound depends on the sampling frequency (increasing the sampling frequency increases the highest frequency that can be carried properly and improves the transparency of the system).

### A. 783

## 取样时钟 sampling clock

A high-precision oscillator used as a timing reference for sampling.

### A. 784

## 取样周期 sampling period

<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="imgs/img_in_image_box_972_1102_1007_1136.jpg" alt="Image" width="2%" /></div>


Time interval between successive sample representations in the digital signal.

### A. 786

## 全电视信号 complete video signal

The combined video signal, synchronizing signals and other associated signals.

### A. 787

## 全频率抖动 all-frequency jitter

Errors in the timing of significant instants of a digital signal, measured relative to the system reference clock, regardless of the rate of variation (all-frequency jitter=wander+timing jitter).

### A. 790

## 热带广播频段 tropical broadcasting band

Broadcasting band reserved for the tropical regions. Note: The tropical bands concern only sound radio broadcasting and are located in the HF band or in its immediate proximity.

### A. 791

## 人工混响 artificial reverberation

Sound effect obtained by processing a sound signal in special equipment, giving the impression of reverberation.

### A. 796

## 三 重播放业务 triple play services

Services that include IPTV, VoIP and Internet Access.

### A. 799

<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="imgs/img_in_image_box_667_404_703_438.jpg" alt="Image" width="3%" /></div>


## 三 维电视 three-dimensional television

Television in which the three-dimensional appearance of the scene is reproduced.

### A. 800

## 三 维预测 three-dimensional prediction; 3-D prediction

A prediction where the predicted value is derived from neighbouring picture elements taken from lines in the same field and in one or more previous fields.

### A. 801

## 扫描 scanning

The systematic exploration of a surface, element by element, in order to produce an electrical signal which represents the luminous characteristics of each element. The process of building up an image on a display device, element by element, these being derived successively from the electrical signal.

### A. 802

## 扫描点 scanning spot

The small area of the target or screen surface, instantaneously affected by the impact of a light or electron beam.

### A. 803

## 扫描行 scanning line

A single line of the picture traversed during scanning (in television).

### A. 804

## 扫描速率 scanning speed

The linear speed at which the scanning spot traverses the surface being scanned.

### A. 806

## 色饱和度控制 saturation control

Gain control in the chrominance path, in a colour television receiver, allowing adjustment of colour saturation.

### A. 808

## 色差亚取样 colour-difference sub-sampling

The sampling grid used to sample the colour-difference signals.

### A. 809

## 色场 colour field

## 基色场 primary colour field

Field produced by scanning in one of the constituent primary colours.

### A. 810

## 色串亮 cross luminance

Appearance of spurious dots on a picture due to the chrominance signal of a picture interfering

with the luminance signals of the same picture. Note: This impairment occurs particularly in systems using composite colour signals.

### A. 815

## 色度路径 chrominance path

Path followed by the chorrininance signal in a piece of television equipment.

### A. 818

## 色度信号 chrominance signal

An electrical signal that is associated with the luminance signal to convey colour information. In practice this signal is made up of two components.

### A. 819

## 色度信号的非线性相位失真 nonlinear phase distortion of the chrominance signal

For fixed values of luminance signal amplitude and average picture level, the non-linear phase distortion of the chrominance signal is the variation in the phase of the chrominance sub-carrier at the output, as the amplitude of the sub-carrier is varied from a specified minimum to a maximum value.

### A. 820

## 色度信号的非线性增益失真 nonlinear gain distortion of the chrominance signal

For fixed values of luminance signal amplitude and average picture level, the non-linear gain distortion of the chrominance signal is the deviation from proportionality between the amplitude of the chrominance sub-carrier at the input to the circuit and the corresponding amplitude at the output, as the amplitude of the sub-carrier is varied from a specified minimum to a maximum value.

### A. 822

## 色蒙罩法 colour matting

A technique, similar in its effect to chroma key which permits soft transitions from background to subject and which also uses colour processing to improve the quality of the final image.

### A. 823

## 色同步相位 colour-burst phase

Phase relation between the chrominance subcarrier burst and the synchronizing pulse.

### A. 824

## 色同步信号 colour burst

A signal comprising a few cycles of a sine wave of colour subcarrier frequency that is used to establish a frequency or phase reference and which may in particular be used for demodulating the chrominance signals and the identification of colours.

### A. 825

## 色同步信号保护间隔 colour burst guard interval

That part of the blanking interval between the trailing edge of the line synchronizing pulse and the start of the colour burst.

### A. 827

## 熵编码 entropy coding

## 统计编码 statistical coding

Method of digital coding exploiting the statistics of the digital signal in order to reduce the bit rate necessary for transmission.

### A. 846

## 摄录一体机 camcorder

## 摄录像机 camera-recorder

Portable apparatus incorporating a television camera and a video recorder and sometimes sound

recorder.

### A. 847

## 摄像管 camera tube

An electron-beam tube for producing electrical signals representing the optical characteristics of an image.

### A. 848

## 摄像机讯道 camera channel

Ensemble of equipment associated with a television camera, including synchronizing pulse generators, amplifiers, a camera control unit and correction devices which allow a complete video signal to be generated.

### A. 849

## 甚高频 very high frequency; VHF

Frequency range between 30 MHz and 300 MHz.

### A. 850

## 甚小口径终端 very small aperture terminal; VSAT

In principle, any earth station having an antenna of 2.5 metres diameter or less. In the EBU/NEC voice conference system, "VSAT" is taken to mean the complete earth-station and associated conference system apparatus (ODU and IDU) installed at a particular CNCT in the Eurovision network.

### A. 851

## 声画延迟 picture-sound lag; picture-sound desynchronization

A time-lag, which is clearly perceptible, between the picture and the associated sound or sounds.

A. 852

## 声音发射质量 sound emission quality

Description for audio quality which is equivalent to or better than good FM service quality or equivalent to or better than good AM service quality.

### A. 853

## 声音广播发射机 sound broadcasting transmitter

Radio transmitter in which the modulating signals represent sound broadcasting programs for direct reception by the general public. The antenna system is often considered as part of the transmitter.

### A. 854

## 声音控制室 sound control room

A room associated with a sound control studio, containing a sound control desk and monitoring loudspeakers and including other facilities such as recording and replay equipment.

### A. 855

## 声音实体 sound essence

A general term for all types of sound essence including audio, MIDI, sampled data, etc.

### A. 856

## 声音无线电广播兼容单边带调制 compatible single sideband modulation in sound radio broadcasting

Mixed amplitude and phase modulation having only a single sideband of bandwidth practically equal to that of the audio frequency sound signal, together with a component at carrier frequency, suitable for reception by radio broadcast receivers, designed for conventional double sideband amplitude modulation.

### A. 857

## 声音信号 sound signal

Audio frequency program signal representing a sound program or the sound accompanying a tele-

vision picture.

### A. 858

## 声音信号电平限幅 limiting of sound signal level

Process by which the gain of a sound signal amplifier is reduced whenever the input signal exceeds a preset level, so that the output signal does not substantially exceed a specified level.

### A. 859

## 声音信号电平限幅系数 limiting factor of a sound signal level

The difference between the dynamic ranges of a sound signal before and after limiting.

### A. 860

## 声音信号动态范围 dynamic range of a sound signal

The difference at a given point of the transmission chain over a given period of time between the maximum and minimum usable levels of a sound signal, expressed in decibels.

### A. 861

## 声音信号动态范围控制 dynamic range control of a sound signal

Control of the maximum and minimum levels of a sound program signal to bring it within specified limits determined by the onset of non-linearity distortion on the one hand and inadequate signal-to-noise ratio on the other.

### A. 862

## 声音信号扩展 expansion of a sound signal

The increase of the dynamic range of a sound signal generally in order to restore to its original form a signal which has been subjected to compression.

### A. 863

## 声音信号压扩 companding of a sound signal

The combination of compression and expansion carried out successively on the same sound signal at two points in a transmission channel.

### A. 864

## 声音信号压缩 compression of a sound signal

The reduction of the dynamic range of a sound signal either automatically in accordance with a specific law, or controlled by an operator.

### A. 865

## 声音信号压缩系数 compression factor of a sound signal

The difference between the dynamic ranges of a sound signal before and after compression.

### A. 866

## 失落帧 dropped frame

Technique used in a digital source synchronizer, allowing the correction of timing errors which exceed the capacity of the buffer memory. If the frame frequency of the external signal is too high, one complete frame is occasionally discarded (“dropped”) to keep the residual timing error within the range of operation of the buffer.

### A. 867

## 失落帧时间码 drop frame time code

A time code numbering system which omits frame numbers to compensate for the variance between nominal fields per second and actual fields per second. For NTSC (field rate approximately 59.94 fields per second), frames 0 and 1 are omitted at the start of each minute, except minutes 0, 10, 20, 30, 40, and 50.

### A. 870

## 时分复用 time division multiplexing; TDM

Transmission of two or more data-streams on a single bearer, each having exclusive use of the bearer for a short period of time.

### A. 874

## 时间和控制码 time and control code

The term “time and control code” encompasses all aspects of the time address, flag bits, and binary groups for user-defined data codes, as well as two methods of modulation of the resulting codewords. It is commonly abbreviated to simply “time code” (note that some users spell this “time code”).

### A. 875

## 时间和日期表 time and date table: TDT

Gives information relating to the present time and date. This information is given in a separate table due to the frequent updating of this information.

### A. 877

## 时间内插 temporal interpolation

Interpolation to obtain the probable value of a signal at a given instant of time, on the basis of the values of two successive known samples, one before the given instant, the other after it.

### A. 878

## 时间偏移表 time offset table: TOT

Gives information relating to the present time and date and local time offset. This information is given in a separate table due to the frequent updating of the time information.

### A. 879

## 时间冗余 temporal redundancy

Redundancy related to the likelihood that the characteristics of a pixel in one frame will depend on the characteristics of the pixel at the same position (or at related positions, defined by known movement within the picture sequence) in the previous frame or the next frame.

### A. 880

## 时间位移 time shifting

A function which allows playback of content after its initial transmission; Act of recording of programd content (i.e. video stream or sound) for the purpose of viewing or listening at other than original scheduled time.

### A. 881

## 时间线 time line

Graphical representation of events scheduled to occur in a predetermined sequence during a virtual editing session. Parameters shown on the time line may include start and end times for an effect, fade-in and fade-out durations, etc.

### A. 884

## 时移电视 time-shift TV

A TV program that has been time shifted.

### A. 885

## 时域抽样 temporal sampling

Sampling in which successive samples are taken from successive fields (or frames) of the 166

analogue picture signal.

### A. 887

## 实况广播引导 guide commentary

A commentary, generally provided in a single language from the venue where the reported event unfolds, for the convenience of other commentators that may be located away from the event venue or may be providing their commentary in a different language.

### A. 889

## 事件 event

A grouping of elementary broadcast data streams with a defined start and end time belonging to a common service, e.g. first half of a football match, News Flash, first part of an entertainment show.

### A. 892

## 视频点播 video-on-demand: VoD

A service in which the subscriber can view video content whenever desired. The operating assumption is that the content is stored on the provider's VoD server. Subscriber accesses the movie from a library directory which may include search engine that accesses movie description and rating. Subscribers typically have the ability to pause, play, rewind, fast forward the content, or even stop viewing it and return to it at a later time when using this service.

### A. 894

## 视频缓存校验器 video buffering verifier; VBV

A hypothetical decoder that is conceptually connected to the output of the encoder. Its purpose is to provide a constraint on the variability of the data rate that an encoder or editing process may produce.

### A. 896

## 视频内插 video interpolation

Technique for reconstructing missing or omitted pictures, or parts of a picture, by using information derived from spatially or temporally neighbouring pictures or parts of a picture.

### A. 898

## 视频信号 video signal

Electrical signal representing the brightness and colour characteristics of a television picture.

A. 899

## 视频信号比特率压缩 bit-rate reduction of a video signal

The processing of a digital video signal to achieve a reduction in bit rate whilst maintaining acceptable picture quality. NOTE-Bit-rate reduction is achieved in source coding.

### A. 900

## 视频信号直流分量 DC component of a video signal

A steady component of the video signal which depends upon the average luminance and in some cases the average values of the chrominance components of the picture, and which may vary from one picture to another.

### A. 901

## 视频序列 video sequence

The highest syntactic structure of coded video bitstreams. It contains a series of one or more coded frames.

### A. 902

## 视频有效载荷 video payload

The picture carried by a digital interface and comprising a matrix of horizontal and vertical pixels. The matrix usually comprises a multiplex of luminance and colour components.

### A. 903

## 视音频内容 audio-visual content

A term used to describe any playable content comprising picture (visual), sound (audio) or data essence and includes any metadata that the content may embed. The content may comprise a single essence element or many essence elements (of the same kind or different kinds) that are interleaved at an appropriate rate.

### A. 904

## 手语翻译 sign language interpretation

A video service showing an interpreter who uses hand gestures and facial expression to convey the main audio content and dialogue to sign language and lip readers.

### A. 906

## 授权管理信息 entitlement management messages; EMM

Private conditional access information which specifies the authorization levels or the services of specific decoders. They may be addressed to individual decoder or groups of decoders.

### A. 913

## 树-枝型系统 tree and branch system

Cabled distribution system having one or more feeders from which subscribers feeders branch at different points.

### A. 914

## 数据传输率 data transfer rate

Average number of bits, characters, bytes, code words, etc. transferred in unit time between a data source and its destination.

### A. 918

## 数据广播 data broadcasting

Transmission by sound or television transmitters of data signals, generally digital, for purposes such as teletext, subtitling and test and control signals.

### A. 921

## 数据块 data block

A basic unit for isochronous packetization.

### A. 923

## 数据流 data stream

A series of data bytes identified by a single stream ID. There are currently two types of data stream in use-essence data, identified by BodySID, and index data, identified by IndexSID. Extensions to the MXF format (either public or private) may add new types of data stream.

### A. 924

## 数据容器 data container

A general-purpose data structure able to accommodate a variety of data formats and suitable for transmission via a variety of bearers.

### A. 929

## 数模视频解码器 digital-to-analog（D/A）video decoder

Equipment used to convert a digital video signal into an analogue signal containing the same information. It incorporates a digital-to-analogue converter and interfaces for the digital and analogue environments in which it works.

### A. 930

## 数模转换 digital-to-analogue（D/A）conversion

A process for converting a digital signal into an analogue signal with essentially the same information  $ [704-22-02\ MOD] $ .

### A. 931

## 数模转换器 digital-to-analogue（D/A）converter

A device for providing digital-to-analogue conversion.

### A. 932

## 数字版权管理 digital rights management: DRM

DRM is a type of server software developed to enable secure distribution—and perhaps more importantly, to disable illegal distribution—of paid content over the web.

### A. 935

## 数字电视互操作性 interoperability in digital television

Characteristics of a digital television system permitting operation on a variety of media. NOTE: Interoperability in the context of terrestrial broadcasting comprises delivery over alternative media such as cable, satellite, VCR and broadband networks, and also conversion to existing analogue TV systems, film and video standards, and interworking with computers and interactive systems.

### A. 936

## 数字电视系统可扩展性 extensibility in digital television

Ability of a digital television system to support and incorporate extended functions and future advances in technology.

### A. 940

## 数字签名 digital signature

A data element that binds a message or transaction to its originator to verify the integrity of the message or transaction.

### A. 943

## 数字视频广播 digital video broadcasting; DVB

A family of standards for digital television broadcasting systems, for delivery in a variety of media: satellite, terrestrial, cable, MMDS, etc. Core technologies of DVB are MPEG-2 compressed video coding and MPEG Layer II compressed audio coding. Picture and sound characteristics can be adapted according to the needs of service providers; DVB includes provision for scrambling and conditional access, service information and other features. Tech. 3274-Part 3-2nd edition.

### A. 944

## 数字视频特技 digital video effects: DVE

## 数字特技 digital special effects: DSE

Generic term covering all picture processing techniques based on the manipulation of digital video signals.

### A. 946

## 数字音频磁带录音机 digital audio tape; DAT

Generic term for digital sound recording on magnetic tape. Often used specifically for the professional R-DAT format.

### A. 948

## 数字音频广播 digital audio broadcasting; DAB

A stereo sound broadcasting system designed specifically to ensure high-quality reception in all listening environments. The DAB system can be configured for optimum performance in terrestrial or satellite broadcasting networks, and for urban, sub-urban and rural areas. DAB uses COFDM modulation to avoid problems of multipath reception in mobile and portable receiving conditions, and MPEG Layer II (MUSICAM) audio processing to provide sound quality similar to that of Compact-Discs with a low transmitted data-rate. The DAB data-stream can be used flexibly, enabling the transmission of full-channel data services, multimedia services, etc. alongside, or instead of, stereo sound programs.

### A. 951

## 衰落 fading

Variation in the magnitude of an electromagnetic field or of the power of a signal due to time variations of the propagation conditions.

### A. 952

## 衰落区 fading area

A region in which fading and distortion occur owing to interaction between the ground wave and the ionospheric wave from the same sound broadcasting transmitter.

### A. 954

## 双声道模式 dual channel mode

The audio mode, in which two audio channels with independent program contents (e.g. bilingual) are encoded within one audio bit stream. The coding process is the same as for the stereo mode.

### A. 959

## 双向预测 bidirectional prediction

A prediction method used in MPEG-2 in which the prediction for a given frame is based on a linear interpolation between predictions from both the previous and the following frames, with compensation for motion estimates. The order of frames is changed so that the following frame is available before the bidirectional prediction is made.

### A. 962

## 水印 watermark

Machine readable data in the form of a signal embedded in a digital media stream so as to be imperceptible to the consumer, but persistent through faithful transformations of the content. Note that this definition pertains to watermarks in the context of IPTV service and is not a universal definition of a watermark. In the IPTV context, watermarks are used to facilitate Rights Management and media piracy investigation.

### A. 963

## 顺序制彩色电视 sequential colour-television

Colour television system in which the components of the signal derived from the three primary colours are transmitted sequentially.

### A. 965

## 搜索范围 search area

Pre-defined area in a picture within which a block matching algorithm tries to find a match (the larger the search area, the more time is needed to conduct a search).

### A. 966

## 素材 material

Material is a collection of audio, video, time codes, data, and synchronization information that may be source or finished content.

### A. 967

## 随机比特误码 random bit error

Isolated errors affecting single data bits, caused for example by noise.

### A. 969

## 随机存取点 random access point

A point in the content from which playback can begin. Note: For example, in MPEG encoding, this would be an I-frame, as opposed to a P-frame or B-frame.

### A. 972

## 损值 impairment unit

Unit for evaluating the subjective degradation of a picture under specified conditions of observation, derived from a reference image which has a medium rating using a given quality scale or impairment scale.

### A. 974

## 索引库 index library

The library that contains all the metadata needed to retrieve and browse the content of the archive.

### A. 976

## 台阶电平 pedestal

The difference in level between the black level and the blanking level of a video signal.

### A. 978

## 特高频 ultra high frequency; UHF

Frequency range between 300 MHz and 3 000 MHz.

### A. 979

## 特技关键帧 effect keyframe

A complete record of the configuration of a digital video effects system, enabling an individual effect to be re-created on demand. The parameters which are memorized may include image sources, fades, wipes, edge treatment, positions of image components on the screen, colours, motion-interpolation modes, etc. A keyframe also has timing attributes and a succession of keyframes can be executed to re-create a complete special effects sequence.

### A. 981

## 提示指令 cue

A pre-arranged signal sent to a studio or other program source for production purposes, to indicate that some action is about to be taken.

### A. 982

## 体验质量 quality of experience: QoE

The overall acceptability of an application or service, as perceived subjectively by the end-user.

### A. 989

## 条 slice

A consecutive series of macroblock rows in a picture, which are encoded as a single unit.

### A. 992

## 条件接收 conditional access: CA

A mechanism by which the user access to service components can be restricted.

### A. 993

## 条件接收表 conditional access table: CAT

The CAT provides information on the CA systems used in the multiplex; the information is private and dependent on the CA system, but includes the location of the EMM stream, when applicable.

### A. 994

## 条件接收解码器 conditional access decoder

Equipment incorporating a descrambler and a conditional access sub-system (CASS).

### A. 995

## 条件接收系统 conditional access system

A complete system which ensures that broadcast services can only be accessed by those who are entitled to receive them. A CA system usually has three main parts: a scrambling system, an encryption system for the electronic "keys" used to obtain access, and a subscriber management system.

### A. 996

## 条件接收子系统 conditional access sub-system; CASS

The part of a conditional access decoder which decodes the electronic keys and recovers the information needed to control the descrambling sequence. May be implemented in the form of a "smart card".

### A. 1000

## 调谐器 tuner

A radio receiver capable of reproducing sound programs, providing only a low-level audio-frequency output.

### A. 1007

## 通用接口 common interface:CI

Standardised interface between a host device (e.g., a set-top box or DTV) and a removable security module.

### A. 1008

## 通用图像格式 common image format: CIF

An image format of  $ 352 \times 240 $  pixels.

### A. 1009

## 通用字符编码标准 Unicode

A form of character coding that allows a wide range of characters and ideograms to represent most major languages.

### A. 1011

## 同步电平 sync level

In a complete video signal the level corresponding to the peak value of the line synchronizing signal.

### A. 1012

## 同步分离器 sync separator

A device for extracting the synchronizing signals from the complete video signal.

### A. 1015

## 同步广播发射机 synchronized transmitter of sound broadcasting

Sound broadcasting transmitter forming part of a synchronized network.

### A. 1017

## 同步数字系列 synchronous digital hierarchy; SDH

Standard data-rates, fixed by the ITU, which allow access to the plesochronous digital networks operated by the PTT Administrations.

### A. 1019

## 同步序列 run-in sequence

A series of unique data words, which do not appear in the normal data, which are used to establish synchronization between the sending and receiving equipment before the start of transmission of useful data.

### A. 1020

## 同步音频 synchronous audio

Audio is defined as being clock synchronous with video if the sampling rate of audio is such that the number of audio samples occurring within an integer number of video frames is itself a constant integer number.

### A. 1021

## 同步字 synchronization word

A unique data word, which does not appear in the normal data, inserted at regular intervals in a data-stream to permit the correct timing relationship to be maintained between the sending and receiving equipment.

### A. 1022

## 同密  simulcrypt

A system allowing scrambled programs to be received by decoders using different access control systems. The entitlement control and entitlement management messages (ECM and EMM) for the different access control systems are sent over-air together and each decoder selects the appropriate set of data for its own use.

### A. 1024

## 同时制彩色电视 simultaneous colour television

Colour television system in which the components of the signal derived from the three primary colours are transmitted simultaneously.

### A. 1025

## 同址取样 co-sited sampling

Sampling structure in which samples for each of the pixel attributes (luminance, colour) represent identical positions in the image. (Note: this does not imply that all attributes are sampled at the same

frequency, or that pixels for each attribute are of the same size; for example, colour samples may be taken only at every other pixel of the luminance sampling structure.

### A. 1027

## 透明比特率降低 transparent bit rate reduction

A bit-rate reduction process that does not affect the subjective quality of sound or picture sequences.

### A. 1029

## 突发误码 burst error

Large number of closely-spaced errors, caused for example by momentary loss of synchronization.

A. 1030

## 图文电视 teletext

Systems which allow the transmission of texts and simple graphics information alongside a normal broadcast television signal. The data-stream carrying the information is inserted in dedicated lines of the vertical-blanking interval of an analogue television signal. The text and/or graphics is displayed instead of, or superimposed over, the normal television picture. Applications include television program information, airport flight information, weather reports, subtitles, etc.

### A. 1033

## 图像编码码字 code word in picture coding

An ordered set of digits representing an element of picture information, e.g. a quantized value, according to a defined code.

### A. 1034

## 图像残留 image retention

Effect seen when the picture content changes and a positive or negative residue of the preceding picture is superimposed on the new picture.

### A. 1035
