## 图像长周期失真 distortion of long duration of a picture

Distortion of a picture, the effects of which are evident during several frames.

### A. 1036

## 图像传感器 image sensor

## 摄像机传感器 camera sensor

An optoelectronic device which produces electrical signals representing the optical characteristics of an image.

### A. 1037

## 图像的短周期失真 distortion of short duration of a picture

Distortion of a picture, the effects of which are evident over a duration distinctly less than the line period.

### A. 1040

## 图像晃动 picture jitter

Jerky and irregular displacements of the picture due to a synchronization fault.

### A. 1041

## 图像开花 blooming

Area of ultrawhite overload much larger than the original image, resulting from the saturation of a part of the target of the camera tube, image sensor or television screen.

### A. 1043

## 图像撕裂 tearing

Intermittent or static shearing of one or more parts of the picture due to a line synchronization fault.

### A. 1044

## 图像同步丢失 loss of synchronization of a picture

Intermittent or permanent disappearance of the whole of a picture due to a frame or line synchronization fault.

### A. 1045

## 图像信号源对比度范围 contrast range of a picture signal source

The maximum ratio of the output levels from a picture signal source.

### A. 1046

## 图像压缩扩展 compression/expansion of a picture

Intentional distortion of a picture by stretching or compressing the picture horizontally or vertically.

### A. 1047

## 图像载波 vision carrier

The carrier which is to be modulated by a video signal.

### A. 1050

## 图像组 group of pictures: GOP

In video compression, the number of frames between adjacent I-frames.

### A. 1051

## 推送式视频点播 push VoD

A TV service where multimedia content is packaged and delivered at the discretion of the service provider to the end-user’s storage system.

### A. 1052

## 拖尾 smearing; streaking

Bands of luminance or colour beyond the normal boundaries of the images of an object in the direction of the line scan.

### A. 1053

## 拖尾测试图 streak test pattern

A television test card for assessing streaking effects in a picture.

### A. 1054

## 外场转播 outside broadcast; OB

A program originating elsewhere than in a studio, using mobile equipment in order to provide a broadcast description of an event.

### A. 1058

## 网络个人录像机 network personal video recorder: NPVR

Same as PVR except that the recording device is located at the service provider premises.

### A. 1071

## 卫星新闻采集 satellite news gathering; SNG

News reporting in which the link between the reporting point and the switching centre or studio centre is by satellite, via a transportable earth station.

### A. 1073

## 未来参考帧 future reference frame

## 未来参考场 future reference field

A future reference frame (field) is a reference frame (field) that occurs at a later time than the current picture in display order.

### A. 1074

## 文档类型定义 document type definition: DTD

A declaration that describes a document type used for XML.

### A. 1075

## 文件传输协议 file transfer protocol; FTP

A standard for finding and transferring files on the Internet.

### A. 1082

## 无损压缩 lossless compression

A completely reversible compression technique allowing perfect reconstitution of the source signal.

### A. 1089

## 无线网络特征 wireless network characteristics

The characteristics of a wireless network expressed in terms of current available bandwidth, packet loss and possibly other to-be-defined wireless network information parameters for a specific wireless link type e.g. WLAN, Cellular, WPAN or WMAN.

### A. 1092

## 无障碍功能 accessibility feature

An additional content component that is intended to assist people hindered in their ability to perceive an aspect of the main content. Examples: captions for the hard of hearing, subtitles in various languages, sign-language interpretation video and descriptive audio.

### A. 1095

## 误码分散 error spreading

Forward error correction (FEC) techniques which cause burst errors to be dispersed in time when decoded, thus enabling their concealment and/or correction.

### A. 1098

## 硒砷碲摄像管 saticon

A low-electron-velocity camera tube with a photo-conductive layer based on selenium, arsenic and tellurium.

### A. 1103

## 下拉变换 pull-down

Pull-down is a process where frame rate is increased through frame or field replication, such as when 24-frame-per-second film is expanded to 60-frame-per-second video.

### A. 1108

## 显示基色 display primaries

The primary colours, usually red, green and blue, that are mixed additively to form the colours of the reproduced television picture.

### A. 1109

## 显示器最大对比度 contrast range of a display

The maximum ratio of the luminance levels available on a display device.

### A. 1110

## 显示顺序 display order

The order in which the decoded pictures are displayed. Normally this is the same order in which they were presented at the input of the encoder.

### A. 1111

## 现场直播 live broadcast

A sound or television program in which the production and transmission are simultaneous.

### A. 1112

## 线性失真 linear distortions

Those distortions that can be caused by linear equipment. Such distortions do not depend on the average picture level, or the amplitude or the position of the test signals.

### A. 1113

## 线性时间码 linear time code: LTC

## 纵向时间码 longitudinal time code; LTC

The acronym LTC refers to Linear Time Code, a codeword format and modulation system which is normally used to record the time code signal on a linear recording medium or to transport the serial signal over an interface independent of any video signal.

### A. 1119

## 向前兼容 forward compatibility

The ability of a system to gracefully accept input intended for later versions of itself.

### A. 1121

## 消声室 anechoic chamber

Room with no appreciable reverberation, used for acoustic measurements.

### A. 1123

## 消隐 blanking

The suppression of the signals conveying picture information during certain parts of the scanning period, for example, during fly-back.

### A. 1124

## 消隐电平 blanking level

The level of a video signal corresponding to the theoretical zero level of luminance.

### A. 1125

## 消隐电平不连续性 blanking level discontinuity

A difference in level between the blanking level during the field blanking interval and that obtained during the remainder of the field period.

### A. 1126

## 消隐期间 blanking period

An interval of time during which picture blanking takes place.

### A. 1127

## 消隐信号 blanking signal

Signal used to control the suppression of the signal conveying picture information during certain

parts of the scanning period, for example, during fly-back. Example: camera blanking.

### A. 1128

## 小型计算机系统接口 small computer system interface; SCSI

A high-speed parallel interface used for connections between computers and peripheral hardware (hard disks, printers, etc.).

### A. 1129

## 小型盘 minidisc: MD

A re-recordable compact disc system for the domestic market. The MD carries up to 140 Mbytes of data, corresponding to 74 minutes of compressed digital audio program.

### A. 1134

## 心理声学模型 psychoacoustic model

A mathematical model of the masking behaviour of the human auditory system.

### A. 1136

## 信道编码 channel encoding

Digital coding for the conversion of a digital signal into a signal that is matched to the characteristics of the transmission channel.

### A. 1137

## 信道编码调制 channel coding and modulation

Processing designed to ensure safe delivery of a digital program or data signal from a source to a destination.

### A. 1140

## 信道均衡器 channel equalizer

Device which stabilizes the amplitude and/or the phase of a signal following digital transmission.

A. 1141

## 信道容量 channel capacity

A measure of the maximum data-rate that can be supported by a given transmission channel.

### A. 1142

## 信号样值 sample of a signal

A representative value of a signal at a chosen instant obtained from the values of that signal near this instant. NOTE-Ideally, the value of a sample is equal to the value of the signal at a chosen instant; in practice, it is equal or proportional to a weighted average of the varying value of the signal near this instant.

### A. 1143

## 信号再生 signal regeneration

A process used in a data receiver to restore the rectangular shape and the timing relationships of the incoming pulses.

### A. 1146

## 信箱模式 letterbox

The use of a picture format to transmit 16:9 aspect ratio pictures, in such a way that upper and lower black areas are added to conform to a 4:3 transmission format.

### A. 1147

## 信源编码 source encoding

Digital coding of original pictures, usually with the aim of reducing the bit rate needed for their

transmission or recording. NOTE-Source coding exploits redundancy reduction, irrelevancy reduction or entropy coding, or a combination of these in order to achieve bit-rate reduction.

### A. 1150

## 信噪比 signal-to-noise ratio; SNR

A measure (in dB) of the relative powers of a signal carrying wanted information and the accompanying noise.

### A. 1152

## 星型系统 star system

## 星型网络 star network

Cabled distribution system, in which all the subscribers feeders originate from the same point.

### A. 1155

## 选择信息表 selection information table:SIT

Used only in “partial” (i.e. recorded) bitstreams. It carries a summary of the SI information required to describe the streams in the partial bitstream. DVB 词汇

### A. 1157

## 循环冗余校验 cyclic redundancy check; CRC

The Cyclic Redundancy Check is used to verify the correctness of data.

### A. 1158

## 压缩 compression

Reduction in the number of bits used to represent an item of data.

### A. 1159

## 压缩比 compression ratio

Relationship between the bit-rates before and after a data compression process.

### A. 1160

## 掩蔽 masking

Property of the human auditory system by which an audio signal cannot be perceived in the presence of another audio signal.

### A. 1161

## 掩蔽门限 masking threshold

A function of frequency and time, specifying the sound pressure level below which an audio signal cannot be perceived by the human auditory system.

### A. 1162

## 眼高 eye height

The height of a clear space in an eye diagram, expressed as a percentage of the nominal data signal amplitude. The eye height is principally dependent on the amplitude response of the transmission channel.

### A. 1163

## 眼宽 eye width

The width of the clear space in an eye diagram, expressed as a percentage of the nominal data signal width. The eye width is principally dependent on the timing accuracy of the transmission channel (synchronization errors, jitter, etc.).

### A. 1164

## 眼图 eye diagram

The “eye-shaped” oscilloscope pattern obtained from the superposition of the signal waveforms from successive time intervals each allocated to one digit.

### A. 1165

## 演播室 studio

A specially designed room equipped for the production of television or sound programs. By extension, can include the studio proper together with its associated technical and production areas.

### A. 1166

## 氧化铅摄像管 plumbicon

A low-electron-velocity camera tube with a photo-conductive layer based on lead oxide.

### A. 1168

## 业务 service

A sequence of events, programs, or data, based on a schedule and assembled by a service provider for delivery to the end user.

### A. 1169

## 业务保护 service protection

Ensuring that an end-user can only acquire content that they are entitled to receive. Note: Service protection is sometimes referred to conditional access.

### A. 1172

## 业务导航 service navigation

The presentation of information that allows the end-user to discover, select and consume services.

A. 1173

## 业务导航接口 service navigation interface

A user interface which is intended to provide information on available services, including content that may be accessed by end-users for service navigation.

### A. 1174

## 业务分量 service component

A part of a service which carries either audio (including PAD) or data. The Service components of a given Service are linked together by the Multiplex Configuration Information. Each Service component is carried either in a Sub-channel or in the Fast Information Data Channel.

### A. 1175

## 业务复用和传输 service multiplex and transport

Method of dividing the digital data stream into packets of information, uniquely identifying each packet and packet type, and multiplexing video, audio and data stream packets into a single data stream.

### A. 1176

## 业务和内容保护 service and content protection: SCP

A combination of Service Protection and Content Protection, or a system or implementation thereof.

### A. 1177

## 业务和内容保护桥 SCP bridge

On a single device, two or more Service and Content Protection systems are operative. Content ac-

required via one Service and Content Protection system can be accessed via another Service and Content Protection system resident on the same device according to granted rights.

### A. 1184

## 业务切换时间 service switching time

The time between the user selection of a new real-time streaming service and the initial display of this delivered service to the end user.

### A. 1185

## 业务群 bouquet

A collection of services marketed as a single entity.

### A. 1186

## 业务群关联表 bouquet association table: BAT

BAT provides information regarding bouquets. As well as giving the name of the bouquet, it provides a list of services for each bouquet.

### A. 1190

## 业务信息 service information; SI

Digital data describing the delivery system, content and scheduling/timing of broadcast data streams etc. It includes MPEG-2 PSI together with independently defined extensions.

### A. 1192

## 液晶显示 liquid crystal display; LCD

LCD is the technology used for displays in notebook and other electronics devices. LCDs allow displays to be much thinner than cathode ray tube (CRT) technology. LCDs consume much less power than LED and gas plasma displays because they work on the principle of blocking light rather than emitting it.

### A. 1193

## 一 次写入多次读取 write once; read many; WORM

A memory device in which data is written once, during manufacture or installation, and read as often as required. (Term commonly applied to CD-ROMs.)

### A. 1194

## 一 维预测 one-dimensional prediction; 1-D prediction

A prediction where the predicted value is derived from neighbouring picture elements in the same scanning line.

### A. 1195

## 一 致性衍射理论 uniform theory of diffraction; UTD

Numerical method for solving electromagnetic scattering problems.

### A. 1197

## 移动性 mobility

The ability for the end-user or other mobile entities to communicate and access services irrespective of changes of the location or technical environment.

### A. 1198

## 移频键控 frequency shift keying; FSK

The instantaneous frequency of the carrier is dependent on the logic level of the modulating data signal.

### A. 1199

## 移相键控 phase shift keying; PSK

A form of modulation in which information is conveyed by changing the phase of the carrier.

### A. 1201

## 因特网编号授权委员会 Internet assigned numbers authority: IANA

The central registry for various Internet protocol parameters, such as port, protocol and enterprise numbers, and options, codes, and types. The currently assigned values are listed in the assigned numbers document.

### A. 1202

## 因特网工程任务组 Internet engineering task force; IETF

The IETF is a large, open community of network designers, operators, vendors, and researchers whose purpose is to coordinate the operation, management, and evolution of the Internet and to resolve short-range and midrange protocol and architectural issues. It is a major source of proposals for protocol standards which are submitted to the IAB for final approval.

### A. 1203

## 因特网协议 Internet protocol: IP

A network layer protocol that defines the addressing mechanism on the Internet to allow data to be transmitted.

### A. 1205

## 音频 CD audio CD:CD-A

Compact Disc Digital Audio format able to record up to 74 minutes of high-quality uncompressed digital stereo sound on a 12cm disc.

### A. 1208

## 音频电平表 program meter

Apparatus for measuring and checking the levels of a sound signal under dynamic conditions.

### A. 1211

## 音频监听 audio monitoring

The operation of listening to programs to assess their technical or artistic quality.

### A. 1212

## 音频控制包 audio control packet

An ancillary data packet occurring once a field in an interlaced system (once a frame in a progressive system) and containing data used in the process of decoding the audio data stream.

### A. 1213

## 音频块 block

A group of 192 consecutive frames. The start of a block is designated by a special subframe preamble.

### A. 1214

## 音频模式 audio mode

The audio coding system provides Single channel, Dual channel, Stereo and Joint stereo Audio modes. In each mode, the complete audio signal is encoded as one Audio bit stream.

### A. 1216

## 音频时钟相位数据 audio clock phase data

Audio clock phase is indicated by the number of video clocks between the first word of EAV and

the video sample appearing at the same time as the audio sample at the input to the format.

### A. 1217

## 音频数据包 audio data packet

An ancillary data packet containing audio clock phase data, audio data for 2 channel pairs (4 channels) and error correction code. An audio data packet shall contain audio data of one sample associated with each audio channel.

### A. 1219

## 音频同步 audio synchronous

One audio channel is defined as being synchronous with another when the two channels are running from the same clock and the analog inputs are concurrently sampled as described in AES11.

### A. 1221

## 音频帧 audio frame

A frame of 24 ms duration which contains information of an ISO 11172-3 Layer II encoded audio signal, corresponding to 1 152 consecutive audio samples at a 48 kHz sampling frequency. It is the smallest part of the Audio bit stream which is decodable on its own.

### A. 1222

## 音频帧号 audio frame number

A number, starting at 1, for each frame within the audio frame sequence.

### A. 1223

## 音频帧序列 audio frame sequence

The number of video frames required for an integer number of audio samples in synchronous operation. As an example, the audio frame sequence for synchronous 48-kHz sampling at 30.00/1.001 frames/s system is 5 frames.

### A. 1224

## 音视频交替 audio-video interleaved; AVI

Technique for the digital coding of video and associated audio signals in a single bit-stream, permitting simultaneous replay when the program component is retrieved.

### A. 1225

## 音视频素材 audio-visual material

Any one or any combination of picture (or video) essences, sound (or audio) essences and data (or auxiliary) essences. This term is also frequently referred to simply as “material”.

### A. 1226

## 音响效果 sound effects

The simulation of real sounds produced in order to provide a listener with particular audible impressions or artistic effects. Note: In English, the term “sound effects” may include effects produced by radiophonic means.

### A. 1227

## 隐含字幕 closed captions

Captions that can be switched on or off by the viewer.

### A. 1229

## 应用程序接口 application program interface; API

An Interface between an application and a particular feature, function or resource of a platform.

### A. 1232

## 用户接口 user interface: UI

Also known as UI, a user interface is the sensory and behavioural aspects of a program that are presented to a user. The term is generally used to denote the menuing and navigational constructs of a program.

### A. 1234

## 用户授权系统 subscriber authorization system; SAS

A centre responsible for organizing, sequencing and delivering EMM and ECM data streams under the direction of a subscriber management system(SMS).

### A. 1235

## 用户数据报协议 user datagram protocol; UDP

An Internet standard transport layer protocol defined in STD 6, IETF RFC 768. It is a connectionless protocol which adds a level of reliability and multiplexing to IP.

### A. 1236

## 游程编码 run-length coding

Data compression technique used to code bit-streams which contain long sequences of identical values. It relies on the fact that fewer data bits are needed to indicate a value and the number of times it is repeated than are needed to transmit every value in the sequence.

### A. 1239

## 有损压缩 lossy compression

A compression technique which is not fully reversible; the degree of residual impairment following decompression depends on the compression technique(s) used in a particular system.

### A. 1244

## 有线分配系统 cable distribution system

A network of non-radiating cables and associated equipment, intended for conveying sound and television programs and perhaps other types of signal to a number of users.

### A. 1245

## 有线分配系统中的馈线 feeder in a cable distribution system

A means of transmission between two points in a cabled distribution system, such as a metallic cable, an optical cable, a waveguide, or any combination of these.

### A. 1250

## 有效格式描述符 active format descriptor; AFD

Defined by ETSI ETR154-a parameter which defines the aspect ratio of the active content within the MPEG coded frame; e.g., 4:3 content within a coded 16:9 rectangle where black bars left and right are part of the MPEG coded signal.

### A. 1251

## 有效行 active line

That part of the scanning line that is not within the line blanking interval, or any line which is outside the frame blanking period.

### A. 1252

## 有效视频 active video

The portion of the video signal that is used to carry picture information. For baseband digital systems, it has the specific meaning of the picture area where the V bits and H bits are both set to 0.

### A. 1254

## 有效视频起始标志 start of active video: SAV

Timing information around a start of active video area defined in SMPTE 292.

### A. 1255

## 有效图像 active image

The portion of the video picture area that is being utilized for program content. Also referred to in CEA-CEB16 as the useful image inside the video frame. Active image excludes letterbox bars and pillarbox bars.

### A. 1259

## 右信号 right signal

The signal intended to be reproduced by the loudspeaker system to the right and in front (of the listener).

### A. 1261

## 右眼立体电视图像 right-eye stereoscopic television picture

The separate picture which is presented to the right eye by means of stereoscopic television.

### A. 1262

## 预测 prediction

The use of a predictor to provide an estimate of the sample value or data element currently being decoded.

### A. 1263

## 预测编码 predictive coding

A method of source coding using prediction.

### A. 1264

## 预测误差 prediction error

The difference between the predicted value and the actual signal value representing a picture element.

### A. 1265

## 预测值 predicted value

Signal value obtained by prediction.

### A. 1267

## 预听 prefade listening

## 推子前监听 prefade listening

Listening to a sound program output, or to elements of that sound program, for control purposes before transmission or recording.

### A. 1269

## 域名系统 domain name system: DNS

A protocol used by the service that maps a host name on a network into its IP address.

### A. 1270

## 元数据 metadata

Data about data. Metadata is structured description of content elements, their relationship, form, related usage rules, obligations and options. Metadata may be embedded in or otherwise associated with the content elements.

### A. 1271

## 元数据格式 metadata format

Identifies the coding format of metadata.

### A. 1272

## 元数据框架 metadata schema

A metadata schema is the representation format for specifying data-model describing target instance.

### A. 1273

## 元数据类 metadata class

The broad category of metadata that forms the first level of hierarchy for all registered metadata.

### A. 1274

## 元数据实例 metadata instance

A metadata instance is the data instance describing the instance of content or user, etc. A metadata instance has its data-model defined by corresponding metadata schema.

### A. 1275

## 元数据业务 metadata service

Coherent set of metadata of the same format delivered to a receiver for a specific purpose.

### A. 1276

## 元数据元素 metadata element

A broad term for a unit of metadata.

### A. 1277

## 元数据注册库 metadata registry database

The standard database of approved, registered data element tags and their definitions.

### A. 1278

## 元数据字典 metadata dictionary

The standard database of approved Metadata Items including definitions and allowed formats.

### A. 1281

## 远场区 far-field region

Also known as Fraunhofer region. The power density decreases inversely with the square of the distance from the antenna.

### A. 1283

## 乐器数字接口 musical instrument digital interface; MIDI

A 16-channel command interface for the control of electronic musical instruments and related equipment.

### A. 1285

## 运动补偿 motion compensation

The use of motion vectors to improve the efficiency of the prediction of sample values.

### A. 1286

## 运动补偿帧间预测 motion-compensated interframe prediction

A combination of motion estimation and prediction which compensates for picture movement that occurs between picture frames involved in the prediction process.

### A. 1287

## 运动估计 motion estimation

The process of estimating motion vectors during the encoding process.

### A. 1288

## 运动矢量 motion vector

A two-dimensional vector used for motion compensation that provides an offset from the coordinate position in the current picture or field to the coordinates in a reference frame or reference field.

A. 1289

## 杂波 noise

Disturbances in brightness or chromaticity that appear randomly in space and time on the picture and result from noise in the picture signal source or the transmission channel, or, in the case of digitized signals, from signal quantization.

### A. 1292

## 杂散光 flare

Unwanted component in a picture caused by the scattering of light in the optical system of the picture signal source or display.

### A. 1300

## 载波间干扰 inter-carrier interference; ICI

Distortion arising e.g. from a lack of orthogonality in an OFDM signal.

### A. 1303

## 载噪比 carrier to noise ratio; C/N

The ratio between carrier power and noise power, usually expressed in decibels (dB).

### A. 1304

## 再次分发 redistribution

The re-distribution of broadcast television content by means different from over-the-air broadcasting, e.g., over the Internet.

### A. 1305

## 再次分发信令 redistribution signaling

A mechanism for signaling “free-to-air” broadcast television content, which is accommodated into the broadcast signal and is intended to prevent unauthorized redistribution of that content over non-broadcast networks.

### A. 1309

## 增强电视 enhanced television

Television system which retains the scanning standards of the existing 625 line 50 field or 525 line 60 field systems, whilst providing various improvements in the quality of the picture and additional features.

### A. 1311

## 增益误差 gain error

An error in the analogue signal delivered by a digital-to-analogue converter caused by incorrect gain setting in the analogue circuits. The dynamic range of the output signal will be greater (or less) than the dynamic range in the digital domain.

### A. 1313

## 占用带宽 occupied bandwidth

Occupied bandwidth: The width of a frequency band such that, below the lower and above the upper frequency limits, the mean powers emitted are each equal to a specified percentage  $ \beta/2 $  of the total mean power of a given emission. Unless otherwise specified in an ITU-R Recommendation for the appropriate class of emission, the value of  $ \beta/2 $  should be taken as 0.5%. (ITU 无线电规则)

### A. 1315

## 啁啾声 chirping

A form of sound distortion or interference characterized by bursts of high-pitched notes.

### A. 1319

## 正极性视频信号 positive video signal

A video signal whose instantaneous value increases when going from black to white.

### A. 1320

## 正极性调制 positive modulation

Modulation where a change from black to white in the modulating video signal corresponds to an increase in the amplitude of the modulated signal.

### A. 1321

## 正交串扰 quadrature crosstalk

In colour television systems, crosstalk between the two components of the chrominance signal as a result of quadrature distortion.

### A. 1322

## 正交频分复用 orthogonal frequency division multiplexing; OFDM

A digital multi-carrier modulation scheme, which uses a large number of closely-spaced orthogonal sub-carriers.

### A. 1323

## 正交取样 orthogonal sampling

A sampling of a picture where the points on the scanning lines corresponding to the sampling instants are aligned in the picture perpendicularly to the scanning line direction.

### A. 1325

## 正向音频信号 positive audio signal

An audio signal is deemed to be positive when it results from an increase in the acoustic pressure on the microphone diaphragm, and thus in the displacement of the diaphragm towards the rear.

### A. 1326

## 帧 frame

A frame contains lines of spatial information of a video signal. For progressive video, these lines contain samples starting from one time instant and continuing through successive lines to the bottom of the frame. For interlaced video, a frame consists of two fields, a top field and a bottom field. One of these fields will commence one field period later than the other.

### A. 1327

## 帧编码模式 frame coding mode: FCM

The syntax element which indicates whether the frame is coded in progressive mode, interlace-field mode, or interlace-frame mode.

### A. 1329

## 帧定位 frame alignment

The state in which the digital frame generated by the receiving equipment has a desired constant time relationship with the frame of the received signal, so that the individual time-slots in each frame can be uniquely identified.

### A. 1330

## 帧定位字 frame alignment word

A distinctive group of digits inserted in every digital frame or once every n digital frames, always occupying the same relative position within the frame, and used to establish and maintain frame alignment.

### A. 1331

## 帧间编码 interframe coding

Predictive coding where the values for prediction are taken from the previous, the current and the following frames.

### A. 1332

## 帧间宏块 inter macroblock

A macroblock that has been coded using information both from itself, and from pictures occurring at other times.

### A. 1333

## 帧内编码 intra-frame coding

Video compression strategies which involve processing within individual frames of the picture signal.

### A. 1334

## 帧内编码宏块 intra macroblock

A macroblock that has been coded using information only from that block or picture.

### A. 1336

## 帧内编码帧 intra-coded frame

## I 帧 I-frame

In compression, a video frame that is encoded without reference to (e.g. extrapolation from or interpolation between) other frames.

### A. 1337

## 帧内插 frame interpolation

The process of creating intermediate video frames (for display) based on the data in two consecutive frames of decoded video. Frame interpolation is not part of the decoding process.

### A. 1338

## 帧频 frame frequency

## 图像频率 picture frequency

The number of complete pictures scanned per second.

### A. 1339

## 帧搜索 frame jog

A function of R-DAT recorders which seeks sounds on a frame-by-frame basis (on an R-DAT machine, one frame is a sound block of 30 ms).

### A. 1341

## 帧跳动 frame bounce

Jitter affecting a television picture in a vertical direction.

### A. 1344

## 帧完整图像 frame complete picture

The ensemble of scanning lines which correspond to the complete exploration of a picture, including fly-back.

### A. 1345

## 帧序重排 frame reordering

The process of re-ordering the reconstructed frames when the coded order is different from the display order. Frame re-ordering occurs when B frames are present in a bit stream. There is no frame re-ordering when decoding low delay bit streams.

### A. 1346

## 帧预测编码 frame prediction coding

Creation of a common set of motion vectors for both fields of a frame. Frame prediction coding may be adequate if the movement within the picture is slow, and this allows a reduction in the overall data rate.

### A. 1347

## 帧周期 frame period

## 图像周期 picture period

The time taken for the scanning of a complete picture.

### A. 1348

## 帧转移电荷耦合器件传感器 frame transfer CCD sensor; FT-CCD

A form of charge-coupled device (CCD) used for image pick-up in video cameras. Electric charges created in the CCD cells (pixels) by the incident light are transferred simultaneously, once per frame, from the light-sensitive layer to an internal buffer memory from which a serial output signal is extracted.

### A. 1349

## 之字形扫描顺序 zig-zag scanning order

A specific sequential ordering of the transform coefficients from (approximately) the lowest spatial frequency to the highest.

### A. 1352

## 直播卫星 direct broadcasting satellite: DBS

A radiocommunication service in which signals transmitted or retransmitted by space stations are intended for direct reception by the general public. In the broadcasting-satellite service, the term “direct reception” shall encompass both individual reception and community reception.

### A. 1353

## 直接预测 direct prediction

Prediction from the both past reference frame (field), and the future reference frame (field) where the motion vectors are derived from the collocated block in the future frame (field).

### A. 1355

## 指配频带 assigned frequency band

The frequency band within which the emission of a station is authorized; the width of the band e-

results the necessary bandwidth plus twice the absolute value of the frequency tolerance. Where space stations are concerned, the assigned frequency band includes twice the maximum Doppler shift that may occur in relation to any point of the Earth’s surface.

### A. 1356

## 指配频率 assigned frequency

The centre of the frequency band assigned to a station.

### A. 1357

## 制式转换器 format converter/transcoder

Equipment for transcoding colour television signals.

### A. 1358

## 质量等级 quality scale

A scale, generally of 5, 6 or 7 steps, making it possible to quantify a subjective evaluation of the technical quality of a picture.

### A. 1365

## 中间件 middleware

A layer of software between applications and resources, which consists of a set of service enablers that allow multiple functionalities running on one or more devices in an IPTV system to interact across a network.

### A. 1369

## 中央控制室 central control room

A room to which program sound signals from different studios or other program sources are directed to continuity control rooms, recording channels, broadcast transmitting stations, or other destinations.

### A. 1371

## 终端用户 end-user

A human being, organization, or telecommunications system that accesses the network in order to communicate via the services provided by the network.

### A. 1373

## 主瓣 major lobe; main lobe

The lobe that exhibits the greatest field strength.

### A. 1374

## 主覆盖区 primary coverage area

That part of the coverage area of a sound broadcasting rransmiuer within which the field strength of the ground wave of a sound broadcasting transmiller is great enough, relative to the ionospheric wave of the same transmitter and noise and interference from other transmitters, for satisfactory reception both by day and by night. Note. —In practice this concept only applies to long-wave and medium-wave transmissions.

### A. 1379

## 主天线 master antenna

Antenna associated with a cabled distribution system intended for feeding the sound or television broadcast receivers of users located in the same building or complex of buildings.

### A. 1384

## 抓帧器 frame grabber

A frame store used to extract single still images from a digital television picture sequence.

### A. 1385

## 拽回操作 pull-back operation

An operation in which a motion vector, which points to a region entirely outside the frame boundaries of a reference frame, is adjusted so that it points to a region which is at least partially inside the frame boundaries.

### A. 1386

## 专家评价 expert viewing test

An assessment session based on the opinions of expert assessors, in which judgements are provided on visual quality and/or impairment visibility.

### A. 1387

## 专家评价员 expert viewer

In a subjective assessment session, a person having a long experience in the area of quality investigation, professionally engaged in the specific area addressed by the subjective assessment test.

### A. 1388

## 转播 rebroadcasting

Receiving a sound or television broadcast and retransmitting the same program simultaneously.

A. 1389

## 转播车 outside broadcast van; OB Van

<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="imgs/img_in_image_box_588_826_624_860.jpg" alt="Image" width="3%" /></div>


Vehicle specially equipped to make outside broadcasts, having recording equipment and equipment for communicating via contribution links or distribution links. Note—The outside broadcast vehicle may be a van, a car, a motorcycle, a helicopter, etc.

### A. 1391

## 准立体电视 quasi-stereoscopic television

Three-dimensional television comprising separate pictures presented to each eye which are derived from a monoscopically received picture.

### A. 1392

## 资料存档 archiving

All of the operations required to introduce new materials into a content library, including verification of the signal quality, generation of backup copies, etc.

### A. 1395

## 子带 sub-band

A subdivision of the audio frequency range. In the audio coding system, 32 Sub-bands of equal bandwidth are used.

### A. 1396

## 子带编码 sub-band coding

A data compression technique in which the bandwidth of the analogue source signal is filtered into a number of non-overlapping sub-bands. Each sub-band signal is transformed into the frequency domain and quantized and the resulting datastreams are multiplexed to create the coder output.

### A. 1398

## 子带样值 sub-band samples

The sub-band filter bank in the audio encoder creates a filtered and subsampled representation of the input audio signal. The filtered samples are called Sub-band samples. From 384 consecutive input audio samples, 12 consecutive Sub-band samples are generated for each of the 32 Sub-bands.

### A. 1402

## 子信道 sub-channel

A part of the Main Service Channel which is individually convolutionally encoded and comprises an integral number of Capacity Units per Common Interleaved Frame.

### A. 1403

## 字符 character

A specific “letter” or other identifiable symbol, e.g. “A”.

### A. 1404

## 字符编码 character encoding

A character encoding is a mapping between an integer input value, and the textual character that is represented by this mapping, e.g. in ASCII value 65 (decimal) is character “A”, or shift-JIS for Japanese characters.

### A. 1405

## 字节 byte

Sequence of 8 bits.

### A. 1407

## 字节对准 byte aligned

A bit in a coded bitstream is byte-aligned if its position is a multiple of 8 bits from the first bit in the stream.

### A. 1408

## 字幕 subtitles

Captions provide a real-time on-screen transcript of the dialogue as well as any sound effects.

### A. 1410

## 自动增益控制 automatic gain control; AGC

A process or device to automatically ensure that the level of output signal remains sensibly constant using the input signal itself as the control.

### A. 1412

## 自然扫描顺序 natural scan order

The scan order in which a two-dimensional array of symbols is scanned row-wise from left to right, and the rows are scanned from top to bottom.

### A. 1414

## 自适应变换编码 adaptive transform coding

A combination of transform coding and adaptive quantization (adaptation according to the relative importance of the coefficients in defining the signal value).

### A. 1416

## 自适应量化 adaptive quantization

Data compression technique which modifies the number of quantizing steps, or their sizes, in such a manner that the system just meets the minimum quantization requirements of the signal which is be-

ing processed.

### A. 1418

## 自适应预测 adaptive prediction

A prediction process which improves performance by modifying the prediction parameters according to an analysis of the current picture content.

### A. 1420

## 综合业务数字广播 integrated service digital broadcasting; ISDB

A broadcasting concept in which several related or unrelated programs or information services are carried in a single delivery channel.

### A. 1421

## 总成信号 ensemble

The transmitted signal, comprising a set of regularly-and closely-spaced orthogonal carriers. The ensemble is the entity which is received and processed. In general, it contains program and data services.

### A. 1422

## 总成信号标识符 ensemble identifier

A unique 16-bit code, allocated to an ensemble and intended to allow unambiguous worldwide identification of that ensemble.

### A. 1431

## 最低有效位 least significant bit; LSB

Binary digit of least significance within a code word.

### A. 1432

## 最高有效位 most significant bit; MSB

Binary digit of most significance within a code word.

### A. 1434

## 左立体声信号 left stereophonics signal

The signal intended to be reproduced by the loudspeaker system to the left, and in front (of the listener).

### A. 1436

## 左眼立体电视图像 left-eye stereoscopic television picture

The separate picture which is presented to the left eye by means of stereoscopic television.

### A. 1437

## AC 系数 AC coefficient

Any DCT coefficient for which the frequency in one or both dimensions is non-zero.

### A. 1438

## AES/EBU 接口 AES/EBU interface

Unidirectional, self-synchronizing serial interface used to interconnect digital audio equipment. It can carry two sound signals with 24-bit quantizing (or less), and ancillary data. The sound may be two independent monophonic signals or a stereophonic pair.

### A. 1440

## AES 音频 AES audio

All of the data, audio and auxiliary, associated with one AES digital stream as defined in AES3.

### A. 1441

## AES 子帧 AES subframe

All data associated with one AES audio sample for one channel in a channel pair.

### A. 1442

## BI 图像 BI picture

A B picture where all the macroblocks are intra-coded. A BI picture cannot be used for predicting any other picture.

### A. 1443

## B 场图像 B field picture

A B picture coded with interlace field coding mode. A B Field picture cannot be used for predicting any other picture except the opposite field of the same picture.

### A. 1444

## B 图像 B picture

A picture that is coded using motion compensated prediction from past and/or future reference fields or frames. A B picture can contain macroblocks that are inter-coded, and macroblocks that are intra-coded. A B picture cannot be used for predicting any other picture.

### A. 1446

## B 帧图像 B frame picture

A frame structure B picture coded with interlace frame coding mode. A B Frame picture cannot be used for predicting any other picture.

### A. 1448

## CCD 取样传感器 CCD sampling sensor

A form of charge-coupled device (CCD) used for image pick-up in video cameras. Electric charges created in the CCD cells (pixels) by the incident light are read in a pattern similar to the scanning raster of analogue television systems (line by line and field by field). The device produces a sampled output signal.

### A. 1449

## CCD 线阵电视电影机 CCD line telecine

Telecine using a scanner in which the film passes continuously over a line of charge coupled device sensors for each of the primary colours which electronically scan the image to produce the television signal.

### A. 1450

## D1 格式 D1 format

Digital recording format for 4:2:2 digital component video and four digital sound tracks on 19-mm (3/4-inch) magnetic tape.

### A. 1451

## D5 格式 D5 format

Digital recording format for 4:2:2 digital component video and associated sound tracks on 12.5-mm (1/2-inch) magnetic tape. It is mechanically compatible with the D3 format.

### A. 1452

## DAB 音频帧 DAB audio frame

The same as Audio frame, but includes all specific DAB audio-related information.

### A. 1455

## DC 差分 DC differential

The DC coefficient of a block in the bitstream that is differentially coded with respect to the DC coefficient of a neighboring block.

### A. 1456

## DC 恢复 DC restoration

The operation of reconstructing a video signal or complete video signal, with its DC component, from a signal not carrying a DC component or from a signal influenced by any standing DC component.

### A. 1457

## DC 系数 DC coefficient

The DCT coefficient for which the frequency is zero in both dimensions.

### A. 1458

## DV 格式 digital video (DV) format

Digital camcorder format. Moving JPEG, compression factor 5:1.

### A. 1467

## I PTV Internet Protocol TV

IPTV is defined as multimedia services such as television/video/audio/text/graphics/data delivered over IP-based networks managed to support the required level of QoS/QoE, security, interactivity and reliability.

### A. 1468

## I PTV 终端系统 IPTV end system

A single or set of consumer devices that support IPTV Services (i.e. everything from Gateway to Display).

### A. 1469

## I PTV 组播互操作性 IPTV multicast interoperability

IPTV multicast interoperability is the exchange of IPTV service information amongst multicast based IPTV service providers. And to make the optimal contract and to provide the stable IPTV services amongst multicast based IPTV service providers.

### A. 1471

## Ⅰ图像 I-picture

In MPEG-2, an intra-coded picture coded using information only from itself.

### A. 1477

## MPEG-2

The standard for the generic coding of moving pictures as defined in ISO/IEC 13818-2.

### A. 1478

## MSC 数据组 MSC data group

A package of data used for one application in the Main Service Channel. MSC Data groups are transported in a series of one or more packets.

### A. 1482

## NTSC 制彩色电视 NTSC colour television system

A simultaneous colour television system using, in baseband, a composite colour signal comprising a luminance signal and two chrominance components, which are transmitted as quadrature amplitude

modulation of a subcarrier.

### A. 1483

## PAL 制彩色电视 Phase Alternation Line（PAL）colour television system

A simultaneous colour television system using, in baseband, a composite colour signal comprising a luminance signal and two chrominance components which are transmitted as quadrature amplitude modulation of subcarrier, and in which, on each line, the polarity of one of the chrominance signals is inverted. Notes: PAL is derived from "Phase Alternation Line".

### A. 1484

## PCM 音频 PCM audio

Linearly digitized audio samples represented in two's complement integers. The integer sample size varies.

### A. 1489

## P 图像 P-picture

## 预测编码图像 predictive-coded picture

In MPEG-2, a predictive-coded picture which is coded with reference to a previous P or I picture.

A. 1492

## QoS 路由 QoS routing

The mechanism that is used to control network congestion and improve network utilization by selecting an appropriate path.

### A. 1497

## SECAM 制彩色电视 Sequentiel Couleur à Mémoire（SECAM）colour television system

A simultaneous line sequendal colour television system using, in baseband, a composite colour signal comprising a luminance signal and two chrominance components each of which is transmitted sequentially, as frequency modulation of a separate subcarner. The receiver is provided with a line period delay line to permit the simultaneous display of the three colour components.

### A. 1499

## T 或 2T 脉冲 T（2T）pulse

Test signal consisting of a sine squared pulse, the mid-amplitude duration of which is T, where T is the approximate duration of the semi-period corresponding to the normal limiting frequency of the video band of the television system under consideration.

### A. 1500

## U 信号 U signal

The colour difference signal corresponding to primary colour blue in the PAL colour television system.

### A. 1501

<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="imgs/img_in_image_box_721_1271_759_1306.jpg" alt="Image" width="3%" /></div>


## V SAT 室内单元 VSAT indoor unit: IDU

The main VSAT equipment unit which includes analogue/digital encoders and decoders, modulators, demodulators, configuration menus of System Generics(SG), plus a power supply.

### A. 1502

## V SAT 室外单元 VSAT outdoor unit; ODU

This unit is attached at the feed point of the parabolic dish antenna. It includes the RF amplifier of the transmitter, the low noise block (LNB) of the receive chain, and the feed horn.

### A. 1505

## V 信号 V signal

Colour difference signal corresponding to primary colour red in the PAL colour television system.

A. 1507

## X HTML extensible HTML

An extended version of HTML.

### A. 1512

## Y-C 信号 Y-C signal

Video signal used in component colour television systems comprising separate luminance and chrominance signals.
